2a1(rgyud): sarba b+hU ta sa ma yo ka d+ha ka
2a2(rgyud): ni 'dzal
2a3(rgyud): na ma ya sa do ra tan
2a4(rgyud): grong / dngang
2a5(rgyud): sangs rgas
2a6(rgyud): thams cad dang ma
2a7(rgyud): ma par sbyor ba/ mkha'
2b1(rgyud): 'gro sgyu ma bde ba'i mchog ces bya ba'i rgyud phyi ma/ dpal
2b2(rgyud): rdo rje sems dpa' la phyag 'tshal lo// sems dpa' sangs
2b3(rgyud): rgyas kun gyi dngos// rdo rje sems dpa' bde ba'i mchog
3a1(rgyud): bzhugs/ 'dir ni rang 'byung bcom ldan 'das// gcig tu
3a2(rgyud): sangs rgyas thams cad mnyam sbyor ba// mkha' 'gro sgyu
3a3(rgyud): dodo pa'i mtsha/ tshugs med chags dang bral pa 'o// dbusangs
3b1(rgyud): mi dmigs so// bud med kun sgyu ma'i rgya// 'di ni gnyis med theg pa'i mchog/ sgyu ma
3b2(rgyud): dag ni thams cad pas// bud med sgyu ma khyad par che// ngo bo nyam kyi mthu dag gis// rang bzhin
3b3(rgyud): gyis ni de grub pa'o// 'jig rten gsum 'dir bud med 'dis// gus par byed pa dag du 'gyur
3b4(rgyud): brnyed dang bde dga' kun gyis// ngan pa spyod pa'ang 'grub par 'gyur// rang gi ngo bo yongs
4a1(rgyud): bsnur nar bud med kun gyis sgyu ma 'grub// ngo mtshar sgyu ma'i phyag rgya 'di// mkhar/ 
4a2(rgyud): 'gro ma zhes bdas stan te// de ni nam mkha' 'gro ba zhes// khams la mngon du brtags pa ste// na mkha'
4a3(rgyud): kun du spyod 'grub pas// mkha' 'gro ma zhes rab tu grags// thams cad ma lus bde mchog gis// 
4a4(rgyud): sangs rgyas thams cad mnyam sbyor ba// mkha' 'gro ma zhes rab tu grags// de ni nam mkha' 'gro ba zhes// 
4a5(rgyud): sangs rgyas khams la rnam par brtags// kun du 'gro ba grub pa ni// sangs rgyas kun bdag mkha' 'gro ma
4b1(rgyud): sham zhes bya ba bde bar bshad// sangs rgyas kun gyi bde chen yin// sgyu ma thams cad rab sbyor ba// mchog tu bde ba'i
4b2(rgyud): bde ba'i mchog/ kun du kun nas thams cad du// bdag nyid rtag tu thams cad kan// sangs rgyas la sogs gtan g.ye
4b3(rgyud): kun/ kun gyi dngos por bdag gyur to// sems dang sems dpa'i ting 'dzin kun// byang chub spyod pa sna tshogs nyid// de bzhin
4b4(rgyud): bdud dang bdud las rgyal// de ni byang chub sangs rgyas yin// rdo rje rdo rje 'dzin nyid dang // de bzhin pad mo pad mo 'chang // ner
4b5(rgyud): bu nor bu 'dzin nyid dang // de dag gi yang rigs yin no// de nyid 'dod chags 'dod chags bral// 'dod pa dang ni 'gro ba'ang
4b6(rgyud): yin da dus gsum srid gsum mchog gsum dang // 'jig rten gsum dang khams gsum dang // rnam pa sna tshogs tha dad pa'i// 
5a1(rgyud): gnas pa'i thams cad de nyid do// 'gro ba dag ni ma lus kun// thams cad du ni 'di 'gyur ro// de las sogs pa mtha' yas mchog/ chos
5a2(rgyud): dbyings mnyam dang mnyam pa// nam mkha'i dbyings kyis mthas klags pa'i// dngos po thams cad de yin te// nam mkha' kun gyi skabs na dpal// 
5a3(rgyud): rdo rje sems dpa' de bzhin gshegs// sangs rgyas thams cad mnyam sbyor ba'i// mkha' 'gro sgyu me bde mchog go/ bskal pa bye ba grangs med pa
5a4(rgyud): sangs rgyas thams cad ma thob pa'i// phyag nA/ 'i cho ga dang ngag gis// tshe 'di nyid kyis thob gyur pa// de ni bdag gis brtag par bya// sa
5a5(rgyud): rgyas kun bdag bde ba'i mchog/ bdag nyid ni na du bsgrub pa las// sangs rgyas kun bdag bde ba mchog/ rnal 'byor yang dag ma yin sos
5a6(rgyud): la dmigs par byed pa dag/ rnal 'byor gzugs brnyan rang bzhin te// gzugs la sdigs pa'i rnal 'byor skye// yang dag mchog sems rnal 'byor pa// 
5a7(rgyud): la rdzogs par byed por dag/ rang gi dam tshig bdag sbyor ba// mi 'gyur dam pa 'grub par 'gyur// gzugs brnyan lugs ma sogs pa la// rnal 'byor
5a8(rgyud): par ma / byang chub sems la rab brtson na// de'ang rnal 'byor lhar 'gyur ro// byang chub sems ni rdo rje ste// sangs rgyas kun gyi bdag nyid yon// dang
5b1(rgyud): cad bdag sbyor bas// sangs rgyas thams cad thob par 'gyur// bdag nyid sangs rgyas thams cad dang // dpa' bo thams cad bdag yin no// de bas bdag nyid lhar sbyor bas// 
5b2(rgyud): bdag nyid rab tu bsgrub par bya// de yis sangs rgyas thams cad dang // dpa' bo rnams kyang thams cad dang // rdo rje 'dzin pa thams cad dang // tshe 'di nyid la bsgrub par 'gyur// 
5b3(rgyud): bcom ldan 'das de pal rdo rje sems dpa' de skad ces gsungs so// sangs rgyas thams cad mnyam sbyor bas// mkha' 'gro sgyu ma'i bde mchog las// de kho na nyid snang ba
5b4(rgyud): pa'i yul la 'jug pa ye shes kyi phyag rgya brtag pa sI dang po'ortsa 'di ni rnal 'byor bcom ldan 'das// rdo rje sems dpa' de bya zhin gshegs// sangs rgyas thams cad mnyam sbyor ba// 
5b5(rgyud): mkha' 'gro sgyu ma bde ba'i mchog/ rdo rje sems dpa' bdag/ sbyor bas// dbab pa thams cad rab tu 'grub// sangs// / rgyas thams cad mnyam sbyor ba// rnal 'byor dbor phyag
5b6(rgyud): bde ba che// de bas bde ba nyid kyis ni// sangs rgyas bde ba kun thob pas// sangs rgyas thams cad minyam sbyor brnal 'byor dbang phyug bode chen po// 'di la khrus dang / 
5b7(rgyud): snga ma mi dgos// dka' thub dka' bar spyad mi dgos// dka' thub sbom po med pa dang // bde ba dang ni dga' bas 'grub// de bas ji ltar 'dod spyad cing // kun ze de bzhin thams cad spyod// skyed pa ci
5b8(rgyud): dgrar 'dod par byed// g.yo ba dag kyang ci dgar byed// langs pa dang ni 'dug pa dang // 'chag gam ji ltar gnas kyang rung // dgod dam rab tu sgra yang rung // gang na ji ltar spyod kyang rung // dkyil
6a1(rgyud): 'khor du yang ma zhugs pa 'am// sgrib pa kun dang ldan yang rung // rang gi lngar ni bdag sbyor na// bsod nams rlung yang 'grub par 'gyur// de nyid rnal 'byor 'dri yis ni// thams cad sgrub pa
6a2(rgyud): byed pa na// ngan zes ngan spyod thams cad kyis// nyes pa dag du yang mi 'gyur// bskal pa bye ba ma'ithob la// sangs rgyas dam pa thams cad de// phyag rgya'i cho ga gong dag gis// bslangs nas kun tu
6a3(rgyud): 'thob 'gyur ba// bdag nyid sgrub par byed pa'i mchog/ dri ni bdag gis brtag par bya// sangs rgyas thams cad mnyam sbyor ba// mkha' 'gro sgyu ma bde ba'i mchog/ rdo rje sems dpa' bdag
6a4(rgyud): sbyor ba// tshwa lugs ji bzhin bsgyur ba'o// thams cad / sna tshogs phyag rgya'i bdag// bsod nams chung yang 'grub par gyur rgyud 'dir srubs pa tsam gyis ni// sangs rgyas thas
6a5(rgyud): cing byin gyis rlob// shin du byin gyis brlabs nas ni/ sangs rgyas thams cad 'du bar 'gyur// sangs rgyas kun dang mnyo sbyor bas// sangs rgyas kun dang mnyam par 'gyur// sangs
6a6(rgyud): rgyas kun dang mnyam par 'gyur// ngas rgyas thams cad 'grub par 'gyur// gang gis ldan pa 'di mthong zhing // rnam pa kun du mchod byed ni// de yis sangs rgyas thams cad kyang // mthong zhing mchod pa
6a7(rgyud): byas par 'gyur// 'di dang sangs rgyas thams cad la// mthong ba dang ni rig pa yis// dkyil 'khor dag du ma zhugs pa 'am// 'den pa dag kyang mthong bar 'gyur// mthong ba dang ni rig pa dang // mthong ba dang
6a8(rgyud): ni dran pa yis// sdig pa kun las rnam grol zhing // sangs rgyas dngos grub thams cad 'grub// 'di dang sangs rgyas thams cad la// rnal 'byor thas cad mnyam sbyor bas// bud med dag kyang rno grol
6b1(rgyud): sangs rgyas byang chub reg par 'gyur// kun tu kun nas thams cad ni// bdag nyid brtag par thams cad du// sangs rgyas thams cad dngos grub par// de yis bdag nyid mthong bar 'gyur// 'di ni bdag nyid kun gnas/ 
6b2(rgyud): pas// mchod pa'i sprin chen thams cad kyis// bkod par tshogs bya ma tshogs dag gis// de bzhin gshegs pa mchod pas mdzes// thams cad bdag nyid sbyor mched dpal// rdo rje sems dpa' mchog nyid ni// sa
6b3(rgyud): rgyas kun gyi rang bzhin te// bde ba'i mchog ni 'grub par 'gyur// rnal 'byor thams cad nye sbyor bas// dpal ni gzhir 'gyur 'grub par 'gyur// rnal 'byor kun gyi bcom ldan 'das// rdo rje sems dpa' de bzhin
6b4(rgyud): gshegs// de yi nye bar sbyor ba ni// khams gsum ma lus thams cad do// rnal 'byor kun gyi longs spyod kyis// ji ltar bde bar bsnyen byed cing // rang gi lha'i rnal 'byor gyis// bdag nyid rab
6b5(rgyud): tu mchod par bya// rjes su sbyor bas mchod byed cing // rnal 'byor kun du bde ba dag/ bdag nyid kun du mya byed na// shin du sbyor bsu 'gro/ ba par 'gyur// sangs rgyas kun gyi bdag nyid kyis// ra sa ya
6b6(rgyud): na bde ba 'dis// rdo rje sems dpa' dpal che dang // lang tsho nad med bde mchog 'grub// kun du kun nas thos cad du// sangs rgyas thams cad mnye sbyor bas// mkha' 'gro sgyu mi bde ba'i mchog/ rtag tu de ni 'grub
6b7(rgyud): 'gyur/ bcom ldan 'das dpal rdo rje sems dpas de skad ces gsungaso// sangs rgyas thos cad mnyam sbyor bas// mkha' 'gro sgyu ma bde mchog las// dpal rdo rje seMs dpa' kun du khe sbyor ba'i rtag pa ste gnyis pa'o// 
6b8(rgyud): 'di ni rnal 'byor bcom ldan 'das// rdo rje sos dpa' de bzhin gshegs// sangs rgyas thos cad mnye sbyor bas// mkha' 'gro sgyu ma bde ba'i mchog/ dpal rdo rje sems dpa'i rnal 'byor pa// dpal
7a1(rgyud): dpal ldan rang gi dam tshig bdam// sangs rgyas thams cad mnyam ster ba'i// rnal 'byor dbang phyug bde ba che// dpal ldan rdo rje sems dpa' sbyor ba yi// mthu nyid kyis ni thams cad du// bya/ 
7a2(rgyud): rgya bde ba chen po kun// so se rjes su rab 'grub 'gyur// dpal rdo rje sems dpa' sbyor ba yi// mthu nyid kyis na thams cad du// rnal 'byor bde ba mos pa kun// so sor rjes su rab 'grub 'gyur// dpal rdo/ 
7a3(rgyud): rje sems dpa' sbyor ba yi// mthu nyid kyis na thams cad du// bde ba mos pa'i dngos grub kun// so so rjes su rang 'grub 'gyur// dpal rdo rje sems dpa'i sbyor ba yi// mthu nyid kyi na thams cad du// 
7a4(rgyud): bde ba mos pa'i dbang phyug kun// se so rjes su rang 'grub 'gyur da dpal rdo rje sems dpar sbyor ba yi// mthu nyid kyis na thams cad du// nam mkha'i dbyings nas mthas klags pa'i
7a5(rgyud): bud med mchog rnams skye bar 'gyur// de'i dam tshig de 'byung ba sdug pa dam tshig bdag rjes 'brang // shin tu sbyor dang / sbyor chen po// thams cad bdag nyid dam tshig mchog/ 
7a6(rgyud): gcig du bzhin du gcig spyod pa// lhan cig spyod pas rjes spyod sdug// sangs rgyas thams cad mnyam sbyor ba// mkha' 'gro sgyu ma mchog du 'bar// thams cad dga' ba ma lus pa'i// phyag rgya
7a7(rgyud): thams cad bde ba che// rtag pa dam pa lha me yi// rgyal mos mchod pa thams cad mchog/ dpal rdo rje sems dpar sbyor ba dang // thams cad lha mo 'dus pas ni// ma lus bskal pa bzang po
7a8(rgyud): kun ta bde bar so sor rjes su 'grub// phyag rgya 'di yis btab pa las// rdo rje sems dpa' che ba'i lha// nam mkha'i dbyings kyi mthas klags pa// lha mo bde ba chen po kun// thams cad rnal 'byor
7b1(rgyud): 'de bas myos// sdig med stobs kyis de 'thon du// phan tshun du ni rab dga' bas// smyos bu'i tshul gyis dgar bar byed// dbang po kun las byung ba yi// mchod pa'i sprin chen thams cad kyis// 
7b2(rgyud): bkod pa rab 'jam sna tshogs kyis// thams cad bdag nyid mchod par byed// rnal 'byor bde ba thams cad kyis// dbang bskur badre chen las byung ba// rin chen mtshogs rnams thams
7b3(rgyud): cad kyis/ rab tu rmongs pas dbang skur 'gyur// lha mo kun gyis longs spyod pa// ci bder bar ni bsnyen bya ba// bdag ni che ba'i lhar sbyor bas// bdag la bdag gis rab tu mchod// 
7b4(rgyud): rnal 'byor thams cad bde ba yi// rjes su sbyor bas mchod byed cing // rtag tu myang bar byed pa na// shin du sbyor// bas rab 'grub 'gyur// sangs rgyas thams cad bdag nyid
7b5(rgyud): kyi ra sau ya na bde ba des// dpal rdo rje sems dpa'i tshe 'grub cing // lang 'tshe nad med bde mchog 'grub// sangs rgya kun gyi sku chen dang // sangs rgyas kun gyi gsung snyan pa// sangs
7b6(rgyud): rgyas kun gyi thugs che ba// sangs rgyas kun gyi mchod pa che// sangs rgyas kun gyi rgyal chen po// rdo rje 'dzin pa kun gyi bdag/ 'jig rten dbang phyug kun gyi gtso// rin chen dbang phyug kun gyi bdag/ de dag
7b7(rgyud): dang ni dga' spyod na// 'dod pa bzhin du 'gro 'ong ldeng // lha mo thams cad grub chen po// 'khor los sgyur bya rab tu 'grub// chos dbyings mnyas dang mi mnyam pa// nam mkha'i dbyings kyi mthas klags
7b8(rgyud): ba ngos bu kun gyi ba mos pa zhinga'i rgya mchog minan med / 'angs rgyam thams cad man mi sbyor badzin po 'byor dbang phyug chen po ngas/ 'dil tsha 'drinang kyis so// ma nga dkun du tho
8a1(rgyud): 'grub pa'i ta dngos grub kun gyi bde mos pa// chos dbyings mnyam dang mi mnyam pa// nam mkha'i dbyings kyi mthas klags pa// dbang phyug kun gyi bde mos pa// dam pa rgya chen
8a2(rgyud): gang yang med// sangs rgyas thams cad mnyam sbyor ba// mkha' 'gro sgyu ma bde mchog des// 'di la tshe 'di nyid kyis ni// rnam pa kun du mi 'grub mod// bcom ldan 'das dpal rdo rje sems/ 
8a3(rgyud): dpas de skad gsungs so// sangs rgyas thams cad dang mnyam sbyor ba// mkha' 'gro sgyu ma bde ba'i mchog las// lha mo thams cad dang rna mnyam par sbyor ba// bskal pa bzang po dpal rdo rje dam tshig gi
8a4(rgyud): rtag pa ste gsum pa'o// / 'di ni rnal 'byor bcom ldan 'das// rdo rje sems dpa' de bzhin gshegs// sangs rgyas thams cad mnyam sbyor ba// mkha' 'gro sgyu ma bde ba'i mtsho/ 
8a5(rgyud): lha mo kun dang mnyam sbyor ba// bskal pa bza' mchog 'dod pa ste/ yang dag sbyor ba'i bde myong ba// 'dod chags ther zug/ btan pa can// sangs rgyas kun gyi gzugs chen dang // dbyangs
8a6(rgyud): dang dri dang ro dag dang // sangs rgyas kun gyi reg bde mchog/ rang gi spyad pas de spyod do// sangs rgyas pha rol phyin grub pa// gzungs dang sa rnams de bzhin du// dga' bar spyod na lha dang mi'i/ bskal pa
8a7(rgyud): bzang bud med ci zhig smos// lha'i dngos grub dga' ba dang // sangs rgyas byang chub bde chen po// bskal pa bzang po byed myong bas// so so rjes su rab 'grub 'gyur// dngos grub thams cad las byung ba/ 
8a8(rgyud): de bzhin gshegs pa kun gyi dpal// bskal pa bzang po'i longs spyod kun// rang gi spyad par de spyod do// rdo rje can gyi grub mchog dang // 'jig rten dbang phyug mchog gi dpal// sangs rgyas dag la mas bde
8b1(rgyud): dam pa ta khrogs nas nye bar spyod par byed// khams gsum dag na ma lus pa'i// sangs rgyas rgyal srid chen po kun// rtsal gyi stobs kyis ngos 'thon du// phrogs nas nye bar spyod par byed// sangs rgyas
8b2(rgyud): kun gyi grub chen po// mchog gi dbang phyug dam pa dag/ kun nas phrogs te de spyod na// longs spyod gzhan lta spos ci dgos// mthu chen las ni bkra shrIs brtan// 'phrog las 'grub dang dran las dga'/ 
8b3(rgyud): ngo 'tho na stobs kyis phrogs nas kyang // de ni dang la sbyin par byed// ma lus 'jig rten gsum rgyal srid// 'jig rten dbang phyug kun dang bcas// ngo 'thon stobs kyis phrogs nas kyang // ngi ni dad pa sbyin par
8b4(rgyud): byed tshangs po 'jug sel dbang chen gyi// mchog gi dbang phyug de rapa dag/ kun nas phrogs te myur sbyin na// longs spyodagazhan lta ci smos// de yi mi sbyin ci yang med// sangs rgyas
8b5(rgyud): don du bya ba kun// mi bya ba ni gang yang med// sbyin pa dang ni byed pa'ang yin// sangs rgyas byang chub sems dpa' yang // phrogs nas kyang ni sbyin byed na// las mtshig dag ni rab 'jam dang // 
8b6(rgyud): dngos grur gzhan lta ci zhig smos// dngos grub mchog ni gdon mi za// sde rnams thams cad rab 'joms pa// sangs rgyas kun gyi grub chen po// 'khor los bsgyur ba rab 'grub pa// sangs rgyas thams cad
8b7(rgyud): mnyam sbyor ba// mkha' 'gre sgyu ma bde mchog gi// sangs rgyas kun gyi rdzu 'phrul che// rnam par 'phrul pa rab tu 'jug/ la lar byang chub sems chen po// la la ri spyod pa 'thun par 'gro// la lar dga' ldan
8b8(rgyud): lha dag los te dam pa shin tu 'pho ba'o// la lar skye ba rnam par dag/ la lar nges par 'byung ba gsal// la lar byang chub chen por gshegs// la lar bdud las rab tu rgyal// la lar byang chub mngon 'tshang rgya// 
9a1(rgyud): la lar chos kyi 'khor lo bskor// la lar pha rol mu stegs rnams// chos dang 'thun par tshar spyod do// la la ra 'jig rten gsum rgyal ba// grub pa kun gyi dbang phyug nyid// la lar rtog pa
9a2(rgyud): thams cad mchog/ grub pa'i dbang phyug bla na med// de la sogs pa mtha' yas mchog/ sangs rgyas kun bdag bde mchog gi// 'dul ba'i thabs su nges pa'i gar// rnam par 'phrul pas dges shing rol// 
9a3(rgyud): dngos grub chen po kun gyi mchog/ brtan pa dbang phyug che ba'i bdag/ gzugs dang tshe dang kha tog stobs// dpal ldan rdo rje sems dpa' bzhin// 'gro ba dag gis bsnyen bya zhing // de bzhin gshegs pa kum
9a4(rgyud): gyis mcho da ha lha mo kun gyis dpal ldan mchog/ rdo rje sems dpa' da rab tu 'grub// sems can khams ni du ma dag/ ma lus param ni phyag rgyas 'debs// lha dang byang chub dka' ba dag/ brtan par
9a5(rgyud): sems can rnams la sbyin// sangs rgyas kun bdag bde mchog gis / sems can kun gyi don byed cing // ma lus lus pa med pa'i bsal ba kun tu srid par gnas// bcom ldan 'das dpal rdo rje
9a6(rgyud): sems dpas de skad gsungs so// sangs rgyas thams cad dang mnyam par sbyor ba// mkha' 'gro sgyu ma bde ba'i mchog las// sna tshogs thams cad kyi bskal pa bzang po mchog gi dngos grub ces bya ste/ 
9a7(rgyud): dpal dam tshig gi brtag pa ste bzhi pa'o// // 'di ni rnal 'byor bcom ldan 'das// rdo rje sems dpa' de bzhin gshegs// sangs rgyas thams cad mnyam sbyor ba// mkha' 'gro sgyu ma bde ba'i
9a8(rgyud): mchog tu yang dag bsgrub pa gcig pu nyid// ji ltar 'dod pa bzhin du sbyar// rtog pa'i cho ga thams cad la// grub pa dam pa mchog gi mchog/ sna tshogs las kyi sbyor ba yis// cho ga sna tshogs 'dod
9b1(rgyud): pA yis/ sems can rnams ni 'dul ba dang // bde ba thams cad 'grub pa'i phyir// bcom ldan rnal 'byor de nyid ni// sangs rgyas thams cad rnam 'phrul pas// sems can don kun rnam 'phrul na/ 
9b2(rgyud): myur du shin tu 'grub par 'gyur// nyi nir 'am yang na zla re 'am// yang na de bzhin le rer ni// ji bzhin byin gyis brlabs nas kyang // sangs rgyas bde mchog gar bya'o// khams kyi ngo bo thams cad pa
9b3(rgyud): de bzhin srog dang brtsol las byung // rang gi lha'i cha lugs su// grub pa'i phyag rgya rab tu bya// dkyil 'khor gang dang gang rten pa// sna tshogs phyag rgya'i mchod po yis// slob ma'i tshogs kun de dang
9b4(rgyud): der mchod pa byas nas der bsgrub bo// de las gzhan yang rmo// kun gyi// sangs rgyas thams cad rnam 'phrul ba// cirigs pa ni sbrul byas pa'i// gtam dag rab tu bshad par
9b5(rgyud): sems dpa' sangs rgyas kun gyi dngos// rdo rje sems dpa' bde ba'i mchog/ gsang ba'i mchog gi dgos pa ni// thams cad bdag nyid rtag tu bzhugs// 'di ni rnal 'byor bcom ldan 'a
9b6(rgyud): rtag pa dmu pa brtan pa ste// rtag tu ltar byung ba bzhin// chog sna tshogs 'dod nams la// las kyi sbyor ba sna tshogs kyi// sangs rgyas rje 'dzin lasags// 'dril ba'i phyir ni byas pa yin// sangs rgyas le / 
9b7(rgyud): pra brtan g.yo kun// kun gyi dngos grub 'di 'gyur ro// sangs rgyas thams cad mnyam sbyor ba// mkha' 'gro sgyu ma bde ba'i mchog/ sgyu ma'i sbyor ba 'di yis ni// rnam pa sna tshogs kun gyi mchog/ sems can kun
9b8(rgyud): gyi don mchog rnams// sangs rgyas la sogs 'dul bas 'grub// dpal rdo rje sems dpas dbugs phyung ba'o// 'das pa'i dus na sngon 'byung ba// bdag nyid chen po brtag pa yi// de bzhin gshegs pas gsungs
10a1(rgyud): rabs las 'gro ba'i tshul ni sngon byung ba/ de'i tshe sems can thams cad ni// shin tu stong pa nyid la brtson// 'gags pa'i chos nyid la sbyor bas// 'gags shing yongs su mya ngan 'das// rnal
10a2(rgyud): byor de bzhin bcom ldan 'das// rdo rje sems dpa' de bzhin gshegs// grol ba thams cad rnam sbyang phyir// sangs rgyas sprul pa kun du bskyed// stong po ma yin mi stong min// dbu mar yang ni mi dmigs te// 
10a3(rgyud): shes rab pha rol phyin sbyor ba// thabs kyi snying rje badrag nyid rnams// de bas de ni snying rje'i thabs// shes rab pha rol phyin par gsal// rtog pa med pa'i chos rnams la// sems can don du yongs rtogs pa/ 
10a4(rgyud): rnam par mi rtog la mos pas// thams cad rtogs pas rtag par bya// brag cha yi ni sgra 'dra ba// chos kyi tshig tu de gyur te// de las theg pa chen po'o// yang dag yon tan rgyas pa'i blas// dus gsum pa'i dam tshig
10a5(rgyud): gsum tu de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad bstod// mnyam med mi g.yo mnyam nyid mchog gi chos nyid can// thugs rje'ibadag nyid 'gro ba'i sdug bsngal sel bar mdzad// yon tan mtha'
10a6(rgyud): yas dngos grub thams cad sbyin mdzad pa// dri med mi g.yo mnyam med ngom pa'i mchog chos can/ g.yon tan shin tu phra ba'i cha ba'ang tshad med de// dpe ni mkha' dang yang bsnun du yod pa min// dngos grub mtha' yang
10a7(rgyud): mnyam med dpa' dang bral ba'i rnams// sems can khams la dngos grub mchog rnams nges par brtsol// rtag pa dri ma med pa'i thugs rje'i shugs las byung // smon lam grub pa 'gug pa med pa'i chos nyid can
10a8(rgyud): 'gro ba'i don grub rab tu brtson pa mtha' yas pa// thugs rje chen po'i bdag nyid rtag tu rnam par spang // tshad med tshad dang bral bar shin tu yongs rdzogs pa'i// bde bar gshegs pa'i go 'phang dam pa brnyes gyur kyang / 
10b1(rgyud): khams gsum khams la dngos grub mchog sgrol mdzad pa yi// thugs rje'i spyod pa mi g.yo 'gag par yongs mi 'gyur// e ma'o shin du bzang po'i chos nyid mchog dang ldan// mchog sbyin rnams kyi
10b2(rgyud): nang na go 'phang mchog brnyes na// khams gsum kun la rtag tu dngos grub mchog stsol mdzad// mgon po dus gsum sgrib pa med par rab mkhyen par// dam tshig mtshan gsum dngos grub dam pa bdag
10b3(rgyud): la stsol/ 'dis ni sangs rgyas thams cad kyi// yang dag yon tan brgyan chen te// lan cig tsam ni brjod pas kyang // sangs rgyas thams cad 'grub par 'gyur// sangs rgyas kun bdag nyid sbyor ba// stod
10b4(rgyud): ba'i rgyal po 'di nyid kyis// dus gsum rgyal ba thams cad kyis// dadam tshig gsum po 'grub par 'gyur// sku ni lta bas mi ngoms pa// thams cad bdag nyid brtan gnas kyang // legs so
10b5(rgyud): zhes ni grub pa yis// mchog rnams kun ni rab sbyin mdzad// thams tshad bdag nyid 'grub dga' dang // bsam pa thams cadayongs su rdzogs// sangs rgyas grub pa mchog kun dang // rnal 'byor
10b6(rgyud): dam pa'ang sbyin mdzad te// de nas de'i bsgrub pa da // shin tu brtag pa'i dngos grub dang // gang gis srid pa 'di nyid la// dngos grub shin tumag thob bshad// rdo rje se gol rtogs pa yin// sangs rgyas thams cad chu
10b7(rgyud): bar bya 'i thal mo legs par sbyar ba yi// thal mo lan gsum rnam par brdab// dbang po gang dang gang lam gyur// de dag de'i ngo bor bya// shin tu mnyam gzhag sbyor ba yis// sangs rgyas kun dang mnyam sbyor zhing
10b8(rgyud): ji ltar dga' mos chags pa dang // bshad pa la sogs pa yis ni// ci nas yongs su ma sbyor bar// rtag tu tshad med bzlas par bya// kun du kun nas thams cad ni/ khadago nyid rtag tu rnam pa kun// sangs rgyas kun dang dngos
11a1(rgyud): grub pa rab tu mthong shing mchog grub bo// 'di yis sangs rgyas thams cad dang // de bzhin dpa' bo thams cad dang // rdo rje 'dzin pa thams cad du// tshe 'di nyid kyis 'grub par 'gyur// sangs rgyas
11a2(rgyud): kyi yon tan bsngags pa brgya che ba// bstod pa'i rgyal po mchog ni lan cig thur blangs pa/ kun du 'gro ba'i rnal 'byor brtag pa'i mchog/ dngos grub mi bzang bde ba thob par 'gyur// bstod pa'i rgyal po 'di yis ni// 
11a3(rgyud): thams cad bdag nyid dbang phyug mchog/ sna tshogs kun gyi rnam 'dul ba// de bzhin gshegs pa kun 'grub ste// de bas dam tshig gsum la sogs// rtog pa bla med thams cad kyis// mamra ma khri'i dbyings kyi mthas / 
11a4(rgyud): papa'i sems can khams ni rnam par grol// dngal ldan rnam pa mdzad da kyi dbugs byung ba'o// 'das pa'i dus na sngon byung ba// bdan nyid chen po brtag pa yi// de bzhin gshegs pa gsung rab la/ 
11a5(rgyud): 'gro ba'i tshul ni sngon byung ba// de tshe sems can thams cad ni// shin tu khro rdum gdug par 'gyur// shin tu gdug cing khro ba yis// 'o dod 'bod pa ltung bar 'gyur// de nas 'phos nas sems can de/ 
11a6(rgyud): bag chags kyis ni mtshams sbyor ba'i// shin tu gdug pa chen por 'gyur// blo ni bdud kyis byin brlabs na// rims dang dug dang dbyig dug nad// phra men ma dag gnod byed gdon// bdud dang rnam par log 'dren nyid// shin
11a7(rgyud): dugadug pa chen por 'gyur// gnas gsum po ni 'jigs byed cing // bsgrub pa po ni kun la'ang za// lha la sogs pa'ang 'pho bar byed// bstan pa dag kyang 'jig par byed// de nas dbang por bcas pa'i lha// tshangs pa'i drung / 
11a8(rgyud): nye ba ra dong ta tshangs pa 'jug pa sel dbang chen yang // rdo rje can la skyabs su dong // de nas bcom ldan rdo rje can// rdo rje sems dpa'i sbyor ba yis// rdo rje se gol phyag rgya ni// sangs rgyas thams cad bsdu bar mdzad// rdo rje
11b1(rgyud): skyems dpa'i sbyor ba'i// dpung ba gzhis no rje bcings de rjes solo gdas papas/ spangs rgyas thams cad 'asrung badzad pa ni/ de'i bka' bas skyes gnas 'khor dang 'khor ra'i rdzogs sa/ 
11b2(rgyud): sangs rgyas thams cad gshegs gyur ba/ gzhan su smos nas kyi zhig dgos// de rje ste go jog pa yis// 'jig chen gsus ni ma lus par// sangs rgyas rdo rje 'dzin bcas pa/ kun gyis thil 'bru bzhin du rgyus
11b3(rgyud): shin tu gdug pa'i gtum po la// zhibs pan par mi 'gyur te// shes rab thabs kyi ngo bos// rje bor de bzhin gshegs kun mdzod// khro bor tshul can khros pas kyang // 'jig rten gsum ni sreg byed na// sangs rgyas thams
11b4(rgyud): cad khros pa yis// khams gsum ma lus spos ci dgos// de bas sna'i be/ daso la// yid ni brtan byar yang dag bzung // sna'i dbugs ni dro ba las// rtul bas phyag rgya'i sbyor 'byor// bcom ldan de yi rnam
11b5(rgyud): 'byor pa jirje khro bor gyur nas byung // dpal rdo rje chen po ga ru ka/ 'bar bas thal par rab tu 'jig/ sems dpa' sngon po 'bar ba'i dang // 'od kyi dkyil 'khor dmar por 'bar// 'jigs pa chen po'i
11b6(rgyud): dus ltar drag/ dur khrod kyi nime dang 'dra// 'bar ba chen po skra 'bar ba// thod pa mang po'i dbu brgyan can// 'jigs pa chen po'i dus ltar drag/ dur khrod bzhin du rab 'jigs pa// khro la sogs pa'i tshul ldan pa// zhal rnams
11b7(rgyud): sna tshogs 'gyur ba dang // smin ma phro nyer bcas par 'gyur// 'bar ba'i lta bas gar bcas pas// gu lang dbang chen nyed da'adu bcas// zhi zla gshin rdza tshangs par bcas// gnas gsum dag ni 'bar byas na// thal ba bzhin du
11b8(rgyud): rab tu 'jig// de ci ma tre ga/ dril bu stani ba'i ma pa'i sa/ thams cad pa ba nas sa mang ni// jal bar 'gyur ba 'dam tsho bar byed/ da'i 'bar pa'i nyam las// 'byung ba'i sring mami bzang pa/ bskyed nas ma lus bdu
12a1(rgyud): la sogs/ bdug pa rnams kyi khrag za nus// rgyal po de ni de dag dang // lhan cig dur khrod rnam par rol// thams cad rdo rje mnyam sbyor ba// mkha' 'gro'i dkyil 'khor ba yis// shin tu gdug
12a2(rgyud): cing khro drag pa'i// sems can khams ni nam sbyangs nas// dag pa'i sangs rgyas zhing rnams su// sangs rgyas byang chub dag la 'god// rdo rje 'dod khrol sogs kyi// rtog pa med pa thams cad kyi// num
12a3(rgyud): mkha'i dbyings kyi mthas klas pa'i// sems can rnams ni rnam par sbyang // dpal he ru kas dbyugs phyung po'o// 'das pa'i dus na sngon 'byung ba// bdag nyid chen po rtag pa yi// de bzhin gshegs
12a4(rgyud): pa'i gsung ra ba la// 'gro ba'i tshul ni sngon 'byung ba// de tshe seMs can thams cad ni// log par lta la gnas par 'gyur// shin tu lta ba ngan pa yis// 'o dod 'bod pa chen por 'byung // 
12a5(rgyud): rnal 'byor de nyid bcom ldan 'das// byang chub sems ni rnam sbyor ba bud mo chags par sbyor ba'i// rdo rje chos su gnas par 'gyuraji ltar pad mo dmar po 'di// 'dam gyi nyes pas mi gos pa/ 
12a6(rgyud): de bzhin bag chags khams gsum gyi// nyis pa sna tshogs rnam por dag/ 'dis ni kun du gzigs pas na// rgyal ba'ang dbang phyug nyid du 'gyur// dpal ldan spyan ras gzigs kyi dbang // rdo rje sems dpa'
12a7(rgyud): de bzhin gshegs// 'dod chags thams cad dag pas na// mchod sbyin dam pas bcom ldan 'das// 'dul ba'i thabs ni sna tshogs kyis// sna tshogs pa'i 'dul ba spro// kun du spyan ras gzigs dbang
12a8(rgyud): rgyal ta pad mo gar gyi dbang phyug gyur// pad mo'i sgyu ma mnyam sbyor ba// mkha' 'gro sgyu ma bde mchog des// pad mo gar dbang la sogs kyi// rtog pa bla med thams cad kyi// na mkha'i dbyings kyi mthas klas bI
12b1(rgyud): sems can khams ni rnam par sbyar// dpal pad mA gar gyi dbang phyug gis dbugs phyung ba'o// 'das pa'i dus na sngon 'byung ba// bdag nyid chen po rtag pa yi// de bzhin gshegs pa'i gsung rab la// 'gro ba'i
12b2(rgyud): tshul ni sngon 'byung ba// de tshe sems can thams cad ni// shin tu bdug cing bkam par 'gyur// shin du 'jungs par 'gyur ba yis// yi dgas rnams dang dmyal bar ltung // de nas 'phos nas slar yang ni// 
12b3(rgyud): shin tu dbul por skye bar 'gyur// bkres dang skom pa'i skyon rnams kyis// de dag phan tshun bsod par byed// shin tu bdug pa sbyang ba'i phyir// rnal 'byor de nyid bcom ldan 'das// dam pa'i don ni nor chen// 
12b4(rgyud): po rdo rje nyi ma shar bar 'gyur// nam mkha' snying po thams cad phyogs/ kun gyi re ba yongs rdzogs mdzad// bud med la sogs rin chen mchog/ mkha' las rin chen thams cad 'bebs// shin tu gdug cing
12b5(rgyud): khro ba la ta zhibs phan par ma 'gyur te// shes rab thabs kyi nyi ma la/ rab tu gdung ba kun bsgrubs pas// bya ba dang ni zlog pa dang / dbrog pas kyang ni khyad par du// rnam par byas na gnas gsuM gyi
12b6(rgyud): nor gyi tshogs kun bsdud par byed// 'jig rten gsum rgyal la sogs kyi// rnyog pa tha med thams cad kyis// nam mkha'i dbyings kyi mthas klas pa'i// sems can khams ni rab tu dkrol// dpa'i
12b7(rgyud): rdo rje nyi ma dbugs dbyung ba'o// 'das pa'i dus na sngon 'byung ba// bdag nyid chen po rtag pa'i// de bzhin gshegs pa'i gsung rab la// 'gro ba'i tshul du sngon byung ba// de tshe sems can thams cad ni// brtson
12b8(rgyud): 'grus shin tu chung bar 'gyur// shin tu brtson 'grus chung ba yis// mnar med pa'i dmyal bar ltung // rnal 'byor de nyid bcom ldan 'das// rdo rje sems dpa' de bzhin gshegs// drag shul sbyor ba'i tshul
13a1(rgyud): dag du k+Sha rtswa mchog dpal ni 'byung bar 'gyur// thams cad dag par mos pa yis// sdig med stobs kyis ngo 'thon du// pha rol gnon pa'i stsal dag gis// shin tu gdug cing khro gtum pa'i// sems can rnams
13a2(rgyud): la mang po'i khams// 'jig rten thams cad rab tu 'jig/ byi ba chom po rkun po yis// thams cad rnam par sbyor bar byed// dri pa dang ni sgyu dag dang // ngo 'thon stobs kyis de bzhin du// dgra cha lnga yis brgal nas ni
13a3(rgyud): detshe 'jig rten kun las rgyal// skye 'gro gnas dang 'gro ba rnams// mtha' dag btul nas 'grub par 'gyur// 'dul ba'i thabs rnams sna tshogs kyis// rang gi rgyal srid rtag tu skyong // g.yem pa rnams las g.yem par 'gyur
13a4(rgyud): khro ba rnams las khro ba'i mchog/ gzhi pa rnams las zhi ba'i mchog/ drag/ shul can la drag po gnon// sdig med stobs kyis ngo 'thon du// dbang phyug dam par rab gnan nas// lha mo b+him phrogs nas ni// de tshe longs
13a5(rgyud): spyod rang gis spyod// sdig med stobs kyis ngo 'thon du// mthu bre che ni rab mnan rtswanas// rug mi med ni phyogs nas ni// de tshe longs skyed rung gis spyod/ sdig mod stobs kyis ngo 'thon du// skye dgu bdag po rab gnas nas// 
13a6(rgyud): lha mo rab tu zhi ba phrogs// de tshe longs spyod rang gir spyod// sdig med stobs kyis ngo 'thon du// 'dod pa'i lha ni rab mnan nas// doga'i stug mo'i dbang phyug ma// phrogs nas de che nyo bar spyod// de la sogs pa mtha' yas mchodag
13a7(rgyud): chos dbyings mnyam dang mi mnyam pa// nam mkha'i dbyings kyi mthasa? klas par// rdo rje las mchog rnam ga/ mnon pa// mkha' kun gyi skabs na dpal// rdo rje sems dpa' rab tu gnos// thabs dang stsal gyis bsgrub pa yis/ 
13a8(rgyud): drag shul sbyor bas bsgrubs nas ni// khams gsum rgyal srid ma lus pa// rdo rje 'dzin pa des 'thob nas// byang chub sems ni mtha' yas mchog/ drag shul sbyor bas bsgrub par byed// thams cad dag par mos pa yis// sdig med
13b1(rgyud): stobs kyis ngo 'thon du// sal gyis pha rol gnon pa yis// sangs rgyas byang chub rab tu 'brel/ lha'i dngos grub dka' ba dang // sangs rgyas byang chub bde chen po// go 'phang mchog ni rtag par dag/ rang / 
13b2(rgyud): gi rnal 'byor gyis thob nas// sems can khams ni du ma dag/ ma lus pa ni rgyas 'debasu shing // mchi med byang chub dka' ba bdag/ sems can rnams la rten par sbyin// rta mchog rnam par sprul pa/ 
13b3(rgyud): yis ta ma lus lus pa med pa yis// bskal pa kun du srid par gnas// sems can kun gyi don yang byed// de ltar rta mchog dpal la sogs// rtog pa bla med de thams cad kyis// nam mkha'i dbyi rjes kyi
13b4(rgyud): mthas gas pa'i// sems can khams rnams rab tu bsgrub/ dpal rta mchog gi dbyugs dbyung dri rmo sogs / mtha' yas mchog/ chos dbyings mnyam dang mi mnyam po/ 
13b5(rgyud): nam mkha'i dbyings kyis mthes klas pa'i// rang 'byung rnams kyi gtam gyis brtags// nam mkha' kun gyi skabs na dpal/ rdo rje sems dpa' rab tu gnas// grub pa'i dbang phyug rab grub pas
13b6(rgyud): thams cad bdag nyid 'jug par byed// sangs rgyas thams cad mnyam par sbyor ba// mkha' 'gro sgyu ma bde ba'i mchog las// rtam gyi rtswa phyag rgya zhes bya ba'i rtog pa ste/ lnga pa'o// de nas gzhan yang
13b7(rgyud): thams cad du// rnam pa sna tshogs mchog 'gyur ba'i// sangs rgyas thams cad mnyam sbyor ba// mkha' 'gro sgyu ma bde ba'i mchog bshad// dpal ldan sangs rgyas kun gyi dngos// rdo rje sems dpa' bde 'byung ba// gsang ba
13b8(rgyud): mchog gi dgos pa na// thams cad bdag nyid rtag tu bzhugs// sangs rgyas kun gyi dam tshig dpal// rdo rje sems dpa' snang ba bdo// de bzhin gshegs pa'i lhar rjes mchog/ rin chen rgyal la sogs pas spras/ 
14a1(rgyud): dril bu rgyal mtshan mchog ldan pa'i// bla re dam pa bres pas na// rdo rje tshig dang mchod pas sogs// glu dang sil snyan rnam par 'phrul// me tog bdug pa'i sbyor ba dang
14a2(rgyud): mor me dril la sogs ldan par// sangs rgyas thams cad mnyam sbyor ba// mkha' 'gro sgyu ma bde ma chog bsgrub// yang na bdag gi gnas dag gam// ma dag bskyed mos tshul la sogs par bsgrub/ 
14a3(rgyud): de ni dang por gnas bshams te// 'jam zhing reg na bde 'gyur ba// sna tshogs pad mo ras kyis g.yogs// de ni thams cad dag pa'i rten// sangs rgyas thams cad mnyam sbyor ba// sbyor ba'i dbang phyug
14a4(rgyud): rnam 'phrul bas// rdo rje sems dpa' dpal gyi lha// de nas rnam par 'phrul par mdzad// stan de dag ni thams cad la// ji ltar gnas pa bzhin du dgod// grub bzhi pa la spro bzhi pa// rtab
14a5(rgyud): bzhis mdzes par byas// rdo rje rin chen pad mo sogs// sgo bsrungs dang ni ldan par bya// rang gi lha dang 'dra ba yi/ bud med dag ni legs sgrub pa// bskal bzangs rang gi phyag rgya mtshan// 
14a6(rgyud): tshogs kyi dkyil 'khor rtag par bya// mi'i tshal ni grub pa la// dmar chen po zhes bya bar bshad// ngo bo nyid kyi mthu dag dang // rang bzhin gyis ni de 'grub pa'o// rdo rje 'chu dang rdo rjer bcas// 'tshal chen po
14a7(rgyud): drag bsgrubs pa ni// mthu yis rab tu grub pa ste// pad mo snod kyi nang du gzhag/ chags pa chen po bcom ldan 'das// rdo rje sems dpa' de bzhin gshegs// sangs rgyas kun gyi rdo rje'i thugs// dam tshig
14a8(rgyud): ni 'da' bar dka'// de'i 'tshal dang khu ba dang // 'tshal chen po ni bsgrubs pa dag/ chags pa chen po les byung bas// dmar chen po zhes bya bar bshad// dam chen po dag ga pur bcas// tsan dan ma
14b1(rgyud): kho sbyar ba dag chos kyi dbus su gzhag pa ni a ra sa ya na kun spang ba// rang gi lha ni sbyor ldan pas// srin lag dang ni 'the bo'i rtses// zhi ba'i btung ba'i bzhin sbyangs nas// rtag pa yi ni dngos grub thob
14b2(rgyud): sangs rgyas kun gyi bdag nyid kyi// ra sa ya na bde ba yis// rdo rje sems dpa'i tshe dang bzhon// nad med pa dang bde mchog 'gyur// sangs rgyas thams cad mnyam sbyor ba'i// mkha' 'gro sgyu ma bde mchog gis/ 
14b3(rgyud): 'dus pa der ni bzhugs pa dang // 'dod pa bzhin du 'gro 'ong ldeng // kun tu kun nas thams cad ni// bdag nyid rtag tu rnam pa kun// sangs rgyas la sogs rten g.yo kun// kun gyi dngos por 'di 'gyur ro// 
14b4(rgyud): 'dis ni bsrung ba byas pas dpal// rdo rje sems dpa' bzhin du'agyur// rnal 'byor mkha' 'gro bde mchog gis/ sangs rgyas thams cad bdag nyid 'grub// de nas khrus byas dri zhim lus
14b5(rgyud): ci 'byor pa'i gos dang brgyan// sna tshogs gos dag bgos nasani// me tog phreng brgyan la dri zhim/ sna tshogs kun gyi bskal bzangs pos// spyong bas dal gyis ngal gyis su// gos dgab pa
14b6(rgyud): yis sbyor ba yis// bdag gi 'byung ba sprul bar bya// rdzogs par sangs rgyas zla rnams// shrI ra ba dag ni mthong bra yis// srog pa kun las grol 'gyur zhing // bsod nams thams cad 'grub par 'gyur/ blangs
14b7(rgyud): pa'i lam dang kun ldan pa// rnam par 'dres pa'o sa rnam par brgyan// rten zhing grub pa spong byed pa/ kun nas slong ba'i bde ba ni// stong pa shin tu rnal 'byor yod med mthus// nam mkha' nyid du dam tshig nye bar
14b8(rgyud): gshegs rta bder gshegs bde ban gshegs pa bzhes su gsol// rdo rje sems dpas bskal bzangs dpal khyod bdag/ 'di dag nyid myi glur blangs na// shin tu mya ngan yongs 'das par// shi ba'ang slar ni
15a1(rgyud): slong 'gyur na// yang srid pa lta ci zhig spos// lam bzhi dang ni mnyam ldan pa// rnam par 'das pas mdzes par byas// sna tshogs 'brang ba rab tu 'grub// 'jig rten gsum ni rab bsgrub pa/ 
15a2(rgyud): 'jig rten gsum gyi phyag byas pas// 'jig rten gsum gyi ston pa po// 'jig rten gsum la sgyid sbyin pa// 'jig rte no gsum po bdag la bu sgrubs// rdo rje sems dpa' dpal 'byor pa/ 
15a3(rgyud): lha mo kun dang 'grogs po yis// sna tshogs kun dang bskal bzangs po// A ra li ni kun 'grub 'gyur// nam mkha'i dbyings kyi mthas klas pa'i// lha mo kun dang 'di mos pa/ 
15a4(rgyud): rdo rje sems dpa' yang dag rdzogs// nyi ma zla ba gsal par 'char// dpal rdo rje sems dpa' yang dag sbyor// mkha' 'gro sgyu ma bde mchog 'byung // lan cig dmigs
15a5(rgyud): pa tsam gyis kyang // bde ba'i dngos grub kun 'byung ba// rten zhing grub pa slong byed pa// sna tshogs 'brang bas de bzhin dedo// gan d+ha ra ba dang shed pa'i// glu brang sna tshogs brus bsgrub po/ 
15a6(rgyud): de nas de nyid dam pa yis// thar pa thams cad rmongs pa yis// rdo rje sems dpa'i bdag nyid la// glu'i yis ni bskul bar bya// rjes su chags pa'i rnam mang dga' ba'i// pad mo rnam par
15a7(rgyud): dag pa'i rnga mchod pas gsal bar rjesu mchod byas pa// mchog tu rtag pa'i rnal 'byor bde bas bde ba 'grub par mdzod// kye ma mchog tu bde ba'i dam tshig ngo bo nyid// mchog tu bde ba
15a8(rgyud): shin tu rnal 'byor bskal bzangs mchog dges pa// rang gi dam tshig skyon med rtag la rol cig rol cig ho// kye ma mchog tu gsang bdag po rang gi dam tshig yin pa'i phyir// rab tu gsang ba'i
15b1(rgyud): lha mo mchog rnams so// 'gro ba'i rgyud ni rnam pa sna tshogs 'dul ba gsal ba mkhyen// dam tshig thams cad dngos po rten g.yo kun gyi ngo bor gyur// rgyal ba kun gyi bdag nyid rnal 'byor bde ba
15b2(rgyud): mkha' 'gro sgyu ma ho// kye ma dam pa rtag pa'i dngos grub chen po rab tu bsgrubs la ston// dza hU~M ba~M ho// e ma bde mchog bde bas drongs// rnam par sprul/ hUM snang bar mdzod// a la la la 'o// 
15b3(rgyud): de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi// mkha' 'gro sgyu ma sna tshogs kyis// slob ma dag ni gzhug du gsol// klu'i rgyal po 'di dag ni// rdo rje sems dpa' dpal la gnas// kun gyi sgyum bde ba'i mchog
15b4(rgyud): ma lus lus pa med par 'grub// glu 'di dag ni len pa na/ dkyil 'khor sna tshogs thams cad du// sangs rgyas thos cang mnyam 'khrul pa// ma lus lus pa med par snang // rnam pa mang
15b5(rgyud): po'i 'dod chags rgyud kyi sems// ma lus lus pa med par 'dul mkhas pa// de bzhin gshegs pa kun gyi sgra ma bde ba mchog/ sgyu mas thams cad rab sprul rnam par sprul// te na
15b6(rgyud): ti te hUM rnam pa mang po rab tu dga' ba'i rgyud kyi sems// me lus lus pa med par 'dul mkhas pa// de bzhin gshegs pa kun gyi sgyu ma bde ba'i mchog// sgyu mas sprul pa rnam par sprul// hU~M hUM hUM/ 
15b7(rgyud): rnam pa mang po khri'i rgyud kyi sems can// ma lus lus pa med pa 'dul mkhas pa// de bzhin gshegs pa kun gyi sgyu ma bde ba'i mchog/ sgyu mas thams cad rab sprul rnam par sprul// ru lu ru
15b8(rgyud): b+h+yo hU~M tA rnam pa mang po srog kyi rgyud kyi sems can/ ma lus lus pa med par 'dul mkhas pa// de bzhin gshegs pa kun gyi sgyu ma bde ba'i mchog/ sgyu mas thams cad rab sprul rnam par sprul// hU~M
16a1(rgyud): Sh+ya bi sha hUM/ de la sogs pa'i mtha' yas mchog/ chos dbyings mnyam dang mi mnyam pa// nam mkha'i dbyings kyis mtha' klas pa// rang 'byung rnams kyi klu'i rgya// nam mkha'
16a2(rgyud): kun gyi skabs na dpal// rdo rje sems dpal la ni gnas// grub pa'i dbang phyug rab grub pas// thams cad bdag nyid 'grub par 'gyur// glu 'di dag ni blangs pa dang // lha mo kun gyis rab skul
16a3(rgyud): nas twa nam mkha' sgyu ma bde mchog gis// sangs rgyas kun gyi bdag nyid 'grub// dbang po kun las 'byung ba yi// mchod pa'i sprin chen rnam bkod pa// rab 'byam tshogs rnams thams cad kyis// kun gyis
16a4(rgyud): bdag nyid mchod par byed// sangs rgyas thams cad mnyam sbyo dab// mkha' 'gro sgyu ma bang mchog gis// dngos po kun gyi bdag nyid lus// ma lus lus pa med 'grub// ston pa'i phyag
16a5(rgyud): rgyabab pa yis// bud mod dag kyang bsgrubs nas ni// rdo rje bcas pa'i mtshan mir 'dzin// rnal 'byor ma ni rab tu 'gyur// de dag rang gi lha rnams dang // 'dra bar byin gyis rlangs
16a6(rgyud): bsgrubs na/ sngon med rol mo'i sil snyan gar// rnam par sprul pas 'grub par 'gyur// lha'i gzugs dang sgra dang dri// ro dang reg pa bde mos pa// bdag nyid rang gi ltar mthong zhing // mchod pa dag kyang
16a7(rgyud): byed par 'gyur// lha'i mchod pa mnyam sbyor ba// bskal bzangs mchog gi 'dod chags can// rnam pa kun du skal bzang po// bde ba yang dag bsgrub par byed// sangs rgyas sgyu ma byin rlabs pas// rdo rje sam
16a8(rgyud): dpa' mnyam sbyor ba'i// dngos grub kun gyi bde ba rnams// dkyil 'khor mthong dka' myong bar 'gyur// rdo rje sems dpa' sbyor ba yi// mthu nyid kyis ni thams cad du// sna tshogs kyis bskal bzangs po// 
16b1(rgyud): rang gi bde ba nyid kyis 'gyu ba sangs rgyas kun gyi gzugs chen dang // dbyangs dang dri dang ro 'de bas// rdo rje sems dpa' bdag nyid kyi// de yis rab mthong mchod pa byed// mchod pa thams cad ma rnam
16b2(rgyud): sbyor ba skal bzangs mchog gi 'dod chags can// sangs rgyas thams cad bdag nyid kyi// dngos grub me lus lus med 'grub// sangs rgyas thams cad mnyam sbyor ba// mkha' 'gro sgyu ma'i bde mchog gi
16b3(rgyud): sangs rgyas kun gyi bdag nyid gar// rnam par rol pa mchog tu snang // de nas yang dag ra nga gsang bas// bud myed dag ni bzhi rnams dang // gur gyi phyag rgya mchod pa yis// mchod pa thams cad dbul
16b4(rgyud): bar bya/ rab tu dga' ba'i bdag la phyag 'tshal lo// de bzhin gshegs pa dam pa grub par mdzod// oM A hUM de bzhin gshegs pa dam pa grub par mdzod// oM a hUM dam tshig
16b5(rgyud): dam pa grub par mdzad du gsol// mchod pa chen po thams cad dag par mdzod// oM a hUMHmchod pa chen po thams cad grub par mdzod// oM a hUM/ klu'i phyag rgya 'di ni dpal// rdo rje sems
16b6(rgyud): dpa' la gnas te// mchod pa ma lus lus med pa'i// rab 'byam las la rab tu rung // gang dag grub par ma gyur dang // mchod la dag ni mi 'byor pa// phyag rgya di yis mchod byas na// mchod pa
16b7(rgyud): thams cad myur du 'grub// mchod pa'i sbyor ba 'di dag dang // lha mo bzhi po dag gis ni// me tog la sogs mchod byas nas// slob ma thams cad gzung bar bya// dngos grub 'dod pa ci 'dod pa'o// snyim pa'i
16b8(rgyud): glar ni kun skyong nas// de dag gdong ni mdzes pa yi// ras kyis g.yogs nas gzung bar bya// dngos grub ji ltar thob 'dod par// slob ma me tog dor du bzhug/ lha mo gang la ltung ba ni// lha dri de la 'grub
17a1(rgyud): par 'gyur te de nas gdong ni dkrol nas kyang // yon gyi mchog ni blang bar bya// sangs rgyas rin chen dbang skur bas// ji ltar bar ni dbang skor ro// dmar chen po dang ga bur bcas// tsan
17a2(rgyud): dmarA po sbyar ba rnams// tshogs kyi dbus su gzhag pa la// g.yon pa mtshan 'dzin rdo rjer bcas// rang gi lha ni rnal 'byor ldan// srin lag dang ni the bo'i rtses// zhi ba'i btung ba bzhin sbyangs mang
17a3(rgyud): drug pa'i dngos grub thob par 'gyur// sangs rgyas thams cad mnyam sbyor ba'i// mkha' 'gro sgyu ma'i tshogs kyis kyang // rgyas mi thebs mi rmongs te// de la gnod par mi 'gyur ro// rdo dris gan
17a4(rgyud): skegs byas nas// sangs rgyas thams cad 'thun pa yis/ mchog tu rtag pa'i bstsal pa dang // dum tshig snyom pa sbyin par bya// sangs rgyas thams cad monyam sbyor cing // snom
17a5(rgyud): pa nyams par khyed byed pa// ji snyed sangs rgyas thams cad dang / byang chub sems dpa' rdo rje 'dzin dang // lha dag dang ni mi rnams dang // de bzhin rnal 'byor 'grub pa po// de dag la ni snying
17a6(rgyud): rings nas// stong la khrag chen 'thung ba zhig/ sems can khams ni ma lus dron// srid pa shin tu dag bya'i phyir// mi 'gog chos nyid sbyar bayis// rtag pa nyid du sgrib par b+ha// bdag gi ngo bo yang smras
17a7(rgyud): shing rtadaka' thub kyis ni gzir mi bya// ci bde dag ni bde bar spyad// 'di ni byi dus sangs rgyas yin// rnal 'byor longs spyod thams cad la// cis kyang mi 'jigs dga' bar gyis// sdig pa med kyis khyed ma 'jig
17a8(rgyud): dam tshig 'da' bar dka' ba'o// grub pa cig pu gcig le spyod// lhan cig spyod dang rjes spyod sdug/ sangs rgyas byang chub bla na med// yang dag nyid kyis rtag tu ston// rdo rje sems dpa' de bzhin gshes
17b1(rgyud): de skad bka' ba stsal dpal ldan gyis// yang dag rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas dang // rdo rje can gyis bka' bstsal lo// rnal 'byor bcas dang gsang bcas pa'i// bdag gis ye shes rgyas sgrubs nas/ 
17b2(rgyud): ci lta'i tshul dang gar byed pas// slob ma rnams la bde ba sbyin// slob ma dam pa de phyin bcad// phyag rgya'i ye shes rjes bzung bas// rnam par snang mdzad mchog bzhin du// sangs rgyas kun gyi bdag
17b3(rgyud): nyid 'grub tu de nas ro dang zas dang gnas// glu dang sil snyan la sogs pa// de dag mgon po rnams la dbul// rdo rje bla ma chen po dang // bdag dang gzhan la 'dod dgus mchod// de nas bdag nyid rab sgrubs
17b4(rgyud): nas twa kun gyi slob dpon rab gnas pa// ji lta'i tshul gyis 'jug pa yis// bden pa'i chos ni brjod par bya// rdo rje sems dpa' dpal gyi tshul// rtog pa thams cad rab 'grub cing // rtog pa kun la rab sbyor ba'i// 
17b5(rgyud): ngo bo nyid phyir chen po'i mchog/ sna tshogs lus kyi sbyong ba dang // 'dul ba'i bdag nyid sna tshogs pas// sems can rnams ni 'dul ba'i phyir// de las gzhan pa'i tshul du bstan// rnal 'byor de nyid
17b6(rgyud): bcom ldan 'das// rdo rje sems dpa'i de bzhin gshegs// thar pa thams cad rnam sbyang phyir// grol ba'i mkha' 'gro byung bar 'gyur// rang gi lha dang 'dra ba yi// rang gi byin brlabs pa sgrub pa'i rgyu
17b7(rgyud): rgyabacing bzhin rjes 'thun pa'i// sangs rgyas sprul pa bsgrub par bya// gzhan yang rnal 'byor bcom ldan 'das// dam tshig la sdang rnam sbyang phyir// thams cad rnal 'byor dbang phyug mchon// 
17b8(rgyud): 'byung bar 'gyur// gzhan yang shin du rnal 'byor pa// ma lus pad mo rnam sbyang phyir// bskal bzang dam pa mi 'gyur ba// pad mo skye ma byung bar 'gyur// gzhan yang rnal 'byor bcom ldan 'das// nor gyi
18a1(rgyud): ni sa snang phyir// rnam pa lnga'i kun kyang dag / ts+li pa byung rgyum nam 'byor do com ldan 'das// rlu shul spyod basbyang ba'i phyig// na 'phrin pa
18a2(rgyud): btan mchog rab tu byung bar 'gyur// rang gi lha dang 'dra ba yi// rang gi byin rlabs sgrub pa'i phyir// gzugs brnyan ngo bor sbyor ba'o// phyag rgya'i sbyor bas gar bya'o// dam tshig rnam pa sna tshogs kyis
18a3(rgyud): de ltar rnam par spyad na ni// sangs rgyas thams cad mnyam sbyor ba// mkha' 'gro sgyu ma bde mchog 'grub// kun du kun nas thams cad ni// sangs rgyas rdzu 'phrul thams cad kyis// bdag nyid rtag
18a4(rgyud): tu rnam pa kun// sangs rgyas la sogs rten gso kun// kun d+hi/ dngos por nge 'gyur ro// kun du sangs rgyas thams na ni// sangs rgyas 'phral pa thams cad kyis// bdag nyid rnam par 'phrul
18a5(rgyud): pa ston te lha mo kun dang 'dus po yis// sangs rgyas zhing ni ma lus par// sangs rgyas sprul pa grub par byed/ sangs rgyas sprul pa sgyu ma yis// sangs rgyas rnams kyi mdzad pa ston/

18a8(rgyud): cad ston par byed// khams gsum pa'i rgyal srid che// bdag po rtul phod pas mnan nas ni// 'gro ba thams cad rab 'joms pas// rta'i gar gyis ston par byed// de la sogs po mtha' yas
18b1(rgyud): mchog chos dbyings man mya dang mi mnyam pa// nam mkha'i dbyings kyis mthas klas pa'i// sna tshogs kun gyi bde mchog gis// nam ma 'a kun gyi skabs na dpal/ rje rje sems dpa' de bzhin/ 
18b2(rgyud): gshegs dpol dgos rol pa rnam 'phrul pa// sna tshogs kun gyi rnam par rol// rnam pa sna tshogs skal brdungs po// rnam pasna tshogs bde mchog gis// 'dul ba rnam pa sna tshogs kyis// sems ca/ 
18b3(rgyud): khams ni rab tu sgrub// de la sogs pa mtha' yas mchog/ chos dbyings mnyam dang mi mnyam pa// nam mkha'i dbyings kyis mthas klas pa'i// sangs rgyas thams cad 'byung ba'i mchog/ nam mkha'
18b4(rgyud): gyi skabs na dpa'i// rdo rje sems dpa' la gnas te// grub pa'i dbang phyug rab grub pas// thams cad bdag nyid grub pur byed// bcom ldan 'das dpal rdo rje sems dpa' de skad ces gsung

18b7(rgyud): rjes su sprug/ dben pa yi ni gnas dag gam// rang gi skyed mos tshal sogs par// kun du sna tshogs bskal bzangs po// kun du sna tshogs 'di mchog gis// kun du sna tshogs dgos pa rnams// ci 'der byar ni

19a2(rgyud): dag par ni grub par 'gyur// rgyal po'i pho brang dga' ba dang // rgyal po'i skyed mos tshal dag tu// rnam pa sna tshogs du ma'i// rgyal po'i dgos pa sgrub par bya// 'khor ni rnam pa sna tshog sla dang // de bzhin
19a3(rgyud): chu bo'i 'gram dag gam// rgyal khams gzhan las grub par ru/ rdo rje ni bsgrub par bya// cha lugs rnam pa sna tshogs dang / sgrub pa rnam pa sna tshogs kyis// dpal rdo rje sems dpa'i dgos pa la/

19a6(rgyud): bkod pa ci 'dra bar// de 'dra'i 'khor lo mchog gis mdzad// rdo rje sems dpa' lha rnams kyi// 'khor lo mngon sum mthong ba las// bsod nams rtag pa ci 'dra ba// phyis dris pa yang de bzhin no//

19b1(rgyud): nyes pa med par 'grub par 'gyur// kun du sna tshogs bskal bzang po// kun du sna tshogs 'khor lo can// kun du sna tshogs 'grub pa'i phyir// kun dkyil 'khor kun du sna tshogs pa'o// dkyil
19b2(rgyud): 'khor zlum po sangs rgyas kyi// rdo rje can gyi zla gam bzhin// pad ma dbang gi pad mo dbyibs// rin chen mchog gi rin chen dbyabs// ji ltar 'dod pa ci 'byor pa// ji lta'i dus dang ci bde bar// 
19b3(rgyud): dkyil 'khor kun du gnas par dpal// rta mchog phyag rgya rdo rje yi'o// dkyil 'khor du ni ma zhugs shing // dam tshig rnams ni spang ba dag/ gsang ba yang dag mi shes pas// sgrub pa ci yang mi 'grub

19b7(rgyud): ba dan te 'dod chags thams cad nam dag pas// skal bzangs spyan ras gzigs kyi dang // log par lha dang ldan pas ni// skal ngan mu stegs 'jig rten nu// dam po'i nor mchog sdud pa'i phyir/

20a1(rgyud): yongs su 'dzin med pas// thub pas thams cad bskul ba ngan// 'dre ba thams cad bdag sbubs pa'i// kun gyi slob dpon skal ba bzang // lta ngan dam tshig la spang ba'i// slong
20a2(rgyud): mthams cad skal ba ngan// gsang ba'i don ni yang dag nyid// 'dir na gsal bar shes pa yis// sangs rgyas kun gyi bka' bzhin du// sangs rgyas kun du 'grub par 'gyur// kun gyi slob
20a3(rgyud): dpon la gnas pas// 'khor lo 'jug par byed pa na// dkyil 'khor 'dod pa'i slob ma la// gsang ba yang dag mtha' yas mchog/ thob pa nyid du gsol brjod pa/ kye'i khyed kyi su la dga' zhes
20a4(rgyud): driHskal ba bzang la bdag dga' zhes// 'jug pa bas kya smra bar bya// gsang ba'i yan lag 'di shes na/ ji ltar 'dod pa rab tu bzhug/ gsang ba yang dag mi shes na// g.yas/ 
20a5(rgyud): pa yis ni bzhug par bya// de ltar dkyil 'khor du bzhugasanas// de bzhin du ni yon phul te// gsang ba'i chog nyid ces pas// mi 'gyur ba'i mchog 'grub bo// kun du sna tshogs bla mal
20a6(rgyud): yon mchog dag ni dbul bar dros// gang la yongs su btang dka' gang // de ni mchog du bshad pa yin// gang dang gang gi sdug pa'i mchog/ yang na shin du khyad par can// de dang de ni bla ma la// de nyid mi zad
20a7(rgyud): 'dod pas 'bul// yang na de ni 'dod 'gyur ba 'am// 'on te sems la dgos pa dag/ de sbyin yang na dgos par bya// de ni chung yang mchog yin no// de ni gal te mchog bdog la// de yang ngan pa'i yon
20a8(rgyud): dbul na ta kun gyi slob dpon brnyas pa na// de nyid rtag tu sdug bsngal 'thob// bu mo shin tu brgyan pa 'am// de bzhin chung ma sdug pa dag/ phul nas rin gyis bla ba ni// sangs rgyas byang chub mchog gi
20b1(rgyud): yin ta mi chan bdag gis phul nas su// slar yang rin gyis blu ba ni// rdo rje 'dzin dpal sbyor ba'i// yon da mchog gi yon yin no// mu tig bzang dang nor bu dang // shin tu dkar ba'i ras zung dang
20b2(rgyud): de bzhin rna ni dkar po dgra// pad mo can gyi g.yon mchog yin// rgyal srid longs spyod gter rnams dang // gos dang rgyan gyi tshogs rnams dang // de bzhin mchod pa thams cad ni// rdo rje nyi ma'i yon
20b3(rgyud): yin no// shin du brgyan pa'i rta drug dang // glang po shin tu rgyan pa dang // shing rta rin chen gang ba dag/ rta'i rgyal po'i yon yin no// khams kyi rang bzhin thams cad dang // srog dang rtsa'i de bzhin ste/

20b5(rgyud): 'gyur dam pa'o// khams kyi rang bzhin thams cad dang / srog dang rtsa ba'i de bzhin de// thod phra rin chen dbu rgyan nam// sangs rgyas gtsug gi nor bu dag/ kun du sna tshogs bla mar ni/ 
20b6(rgyud): kun du slob dpon ku nu la bya// rgyal sred thams cad nam dag la// ma lus lus pa med par 'grub// rin rkyen ngo mtshong gicag las byas// de bzhin sna tshogs rgya rI gyis smras// sangs rgyas par po
20b7(rgyud): dbang skyer byas// sgrib ma thams cad dbang sbyar ro// sangs rgyas rin chen rdo rje byed// rdo rje'i rigs la rdo rje yin// spyan ras gzigs kyi rdo rje sku/ ning bu 'dzin gyi nor bu yin// sangs rgyas rin
20b8(rgyud): chen pad mo dang // rdo rje nor bu de bzhin du// thams cad mchog ni rta mchog lo// rang gi dbang skur sdus pa'o// blugs pa 'am ni byas pa 'am/ rdung ba'am ni bris kyang rung // sna tshogs rab tu
21a1(rgyud): legs pa ying mtshan ma'i phyag rngu rab tu dag/ kun du sna tshogs bskul bzangs po// rang 'byung rnams kyi mtshan ma'i rgya/ tham mkha'i dbyings kyi sa thas klas pa'i// lha mamam
21a2(rgyud): kyi bde ba mchog/ gzhu dang mda' dang de bzhin du// skal ba'ang de ni bskal pa bzang // thod pa dang ni khA trAM khA/ rdo rje n+ya grum de bzhin no// bad mo rgya gram dpag med tshe'i// sangs rgyas kun gyi tshe smra
21a3(rgyud): lha mo tshogs rnams thams cad kyi// mtshan ma'i phyag rgya tshogs bsgrubs bzhin// mda' dang de bzhin tshangs pa'i 'gro// de bzhin 'khor lo'i phyag rgya dang // rdo rje dril shul phyag rgya'i mtshan// dpag pas
21a4(rgyud): shing dang lkug pa dang // pad mo rta 'grin 'phang 'tho ba// rta 'grin ljang gu de bzhin no// phag gi 'che ba grub pa dang // zla ba nyi ma de bzhin no// rin chen sna tshogs snod chen du// sangs rgyas
21a5(rgyud): gzugs kyi ra sa yan// thams cad bdag nyid myong skal bzang // metshan ma'i phyag rgya sna tshogs gzhag/ gling bu dang ni pi wang kun// ku mA ta dang mu ra dzA// me tog gdug pa mar me dang
21a6(rgyud): sna tshogs dri rnams de bzhin no// de la sogs te mtha' yas mchog/ chos dbyings mnyam dang mi mnyam pa// nam mkha'i dbyings kyi mthas klas pa'i// mtshan ma'i phyag rgya dam po'i tshogs/ 
21a7(rgyud): nam mkha' kun gyi skabs na dpral// rdo rje sems dpa' nyid la gnas/ grub pa'i dbang phyug rab grub pas// thams cad bo dag nyid grub par 'gyur// chos gos dang ni ltung zed dang // de bzhin
21a8(rgyud): du ni mkhar sil dang // dam pa'i chos kyi glegs bam dag/ mtshan ma'i phyag rgya'i tshogs gzhan no// de bzhin lce'i phyag rgya dang // cha lang dang ni rnga dag dang // rdo rje dang ni rin chen snod// mtshan
21b1(rgyud): ma'i phyag rgyas gos gzhan no// de bzhin sangs rgyas gzugs brnyan dang // me long drang ni rlung yang dang // rdo rje ser ba'i sprin dang bcas// de bzhin mig gi phyag rgya dang // rdo rje 'bar dang khAN+Da
21b2(rgyud): ga thod pa kham dang de bzhin no// dmar chen dbo snying chen dang // sha chen po yang de bzhin te// rnon po 'da' dang de bzhin 'dren// chang dang chu dang de bzhin te// lcug ma rlung gis skyod pa dang // ras dang
21b3(rgyud): de bzhin me dag ni// rdo rje khro bo'i rgya po'i dpal// bdug pa thams cad za ba yi// mtshan ma'i phyag rgya grub pa'i tshogs// rnal 'byor dngos grub rab spungs pa'o// khang mo sna tshogs dmar po dang / 
21b4(rgyud): ljang gu de bzhin dkar po dang // mthing ka ser po le rgan dang // pad ma'i mtshan mchog rnam po bdun// ba ma sprang po bud ma de bzhini chos kyi 'khor lo dang // gsal shing dpal sreng rdo rje
21b5(rgyud): dag ta par mo mtshan ma'i tshogs gzhan no// gzhu dang mda' dang ral gri dang // de bzhin du ni 'bar ba'i me// dbang skur btwe dang rgyal mtshan dag/ mchod pa'i mtshan ma sdus pa'o// 
21b6(rgyud): bzhin sna tshogs dang mo dang // rdo rje n+ya rje de bzhin te// mtshon ma'i phyag rgya 'grub pa gnyis// rgyal srid thams cad 'joms pa ste// sangs rgyas thams cad la sogs pa// dngos po brtan g.yo ma lus kun
21b7(rgyud): rang 'byung rnams ni mtshan min+tu// rnam ma'i'i dbyings kyi mthas thos pa'o// de skad bcom ldan de bzhin gshegs// rdo rje sems dpa' dpal gyis gsungs// sangs rgyas thams cad mamam par sgo
21b8(rgyud): gamangar 'gro sgyum bde ba'i mchog las/ dkyil 'khor thams cad kyi phyag rgya zhes pa'i rtog pa ste 'du ba sgo/ de nas gnan mang bshang ba 'dzi'i sems dpa' dpal gyis/ ram du TI
22a1(rgyud): tshogs kyi mchog/ mchod pa thams cad rnam sprul pa// lug pa gams gson gnyis dag gis// 'dzub mo ze'u chung mdzes par sbyar// dpal ldan g.yon pa 'gying ba'i thabs/ blagayas
22a2(rgyud): pra ba dan gsum par bya// sre gzur gyur pa'i sreg pa'i mchog/ bdag nyid rdo rje sems dpa' dang la// 'dzub dang bcas pa'i tshig gis lha// bsam pa g.yos pa'i phyag rgya'o// sangs rgyas rdo rje bangs
22a3(rgyud): 'dzin rdo rje tshom khams gsum pas// skad cig gis kyang phyag byed na// khengs bya gzhan ci nig smos// drag po dbang po ni dbang bcas// nyi zla gshin rje tshangs par bcas/ bdud te rab tu byas
22a4(rgyud): 'tshal nas tA las rnams thams cad byed par 'gyur// rdo rje dpal gyi thal mo sbyar// bsam pa g.yos pas phyag byas pa'isangs rgyas mchod pa legs byas nas// ma lus lus pa med
22a5(rgyud): par 'grub tu smin ma g.yon ma rdeg tshul gyis// ru lu ru lur bcas dgad na// tshangs pa nye dbang drag po bcas// khams gsum pa rnams phyag byed 'gyur// thal mo padad+ma mo kha 'bus bzhin
22a6(rgyud): rang nyid sbyor ldan snying kar bcas// 'the bo 'the chung 'dab ma bzhin// rgyas pa btud pa'i phyag rgya bya// lus kyi yan lag thams cad ni// sa la stel te phyag bya ba// snying ka dang ni spyi gtsug tu// thal mo
22a7(rgyud): sbyar te drug bya'o// dpal ldan rdo rje 'gyeng ba'i thabs// 'dzum pa'i mig gis phyag byas nas// khams gsum po sang phrag byed na// mthung sems gzhan lnga ci nig spos// phyag rgya 'tshal ba'i phyag rgyar
22a8(rgyud): shes pa'i ti gar gyi rgyud rnams ji snyed pa'o// de bzhin bya ba'i tshul ston kun// de dag rdo rje sems dpa'i rgya// rang gi don rnams 'grub byed pa'o// 'gying dang bcas pa'i tshul byas nas// ji ltar tshul bzhen/ 
22b1(rgyud): gar byed cing skor ba'i gar rnams sna tshogs kyis// mchod pa sna tshogs dbul bar bya// lag pa g.yas g.yon gnyis dag gis// 'dzub po 'the'u chung mdzes bsgyur te// g.yon pa'i 'dzub mo
22b2(rgyud): khur tshur bcas// g.yas pa ba dan gsum par bya// phyag rgya 'di yis btab na ni// sangs rgyas kun dang 'grogs pa dang // dngos grub chen po mchog kun gyi// dbang phyug chen po 'grub par 'gyur
22b3(rgyud): sangs rgyas thams cad dang 'grogs pa// dpal bskal po bzang po zhes bya ba'i phyag rgya'o// snyems 'dzin chen por bcas pa yi// sbyor bas de ni bteg nas su// 'gram pa'i phyogs su yongs
22b4(rgyud): sbyar nas ta spyi bo mtshams su gzhag par bya// thams cad 'bebaso pa'i gor byed pas// gar byas de nus phab nas su / skal bzang hUM zhes khyab pa'i klus// mchod pa thams cad
22b5(rgyud): dbul bar bya// sangs rgyas thams cad mnyam skyo ra ba// dpal bzang po bde ba chen po zhes bya ba'i phyag rgya'o// lag pa g.yas g.yon gnyis dag gis// 'dzub mo 'the'u chung mdzes sbyar
22b6(rgyud): bo'i te rdo rje thal mo sbyar nas su// de bzhin g.yon du sbyar bar byas// de ni sbyor bas bteg nas ni// spyi'i'i mtshams su gzhag par bya// skal bzang oM zhes bya ba'i glus// mchod pa thams cad
22b7(rgyud): dbul bar bya// dpol rdo rje thal mo sbyar ba sangs rgyas kyis mchod pa'o// lag pa g.yas g.yon gonyis dag gis// 'dzub mo 'the'u mdzes sbyar te// rdo rje thol mo gyen du grol// mchod pa'i rtor
22b8(rgyud): ma kun gyi tshul ta dur khrod cha lugs gar byed pas// phyag rgya 'di yis gar byed cing // skal bzangs rdo rje drag por 'god// mchod pa thams cad dbul bar bya// dpal rdo rje he ru ka'i thal mo ste/ 
23a1(rgyud): mchod pa'i gtor ma thams cad kyi cho ga'o// lag pa g.yas g.yon gnyis dag gis// 'dzub mo 'the'u chung mdzes sbyar te// rdo rje rin chen thal sbyar nas// marjod pa
23a2(rgyud): thams cad dbul bar bya// rje ba thams cad yongs su rdzogs par byed pa// dpal rdo rje rin chen zhes bya ba'i phyag rgya'o// gyen du 'thor zhing 'thur du 'bebs// skor zhing de bzhin
23a3(rgyud): zhug pa dang / me tog gdug pa'i mar me mchog/ dri'i mchod pa 'byung ba'o// gang ba'am 'on te stong pa yang rung // yang na ci 'byor pa yis kyang // dam tshig nyams par sgrubs pa yis
23a4(rgyud): mchod pa thams cad 'grub par 'gyur// phyag rgya 'di rnams bcings nas ni// sangs rgyas thams cad mchod para'o// gyur// dngos grub dbang phyug grub pas kyang / 
23a5(rgyud): kun gyi bdag nyid mchod par 'gyur// chos dbyings mnyam dang mi mnyam pa// nam mkha'i dbyings kyis mthas klas pa'i// rang 'byung rnams kyi mchod pa kun// gang
23a6(rgyud): dag de yis ma byas shing // spel bar yang nI ma gyur ba'i// rlabs chen dam pa gang yang med// sangs rgyas thams cad mnyam sbyor ba// 'byor pa'i dbang phyug bde chen dang / 
23a7(rgyud): dngos grub las dang bde bdag/ 'di yis mi 'grub gang yang med// mchod pa rab 'byam 'grub pa rnams// ma lus lus pa sod par grub ces dpal// bcom ldan 'das
23a8(rgyud): sems depas gsungs// sangs rgyas thams cad chegs sbyor ga/ mkha' 'gro sum 'de pa'i mtshig mas thams cad marnam par byor ga// dpa la skam pa pabang po'i
23b1(rgyud): tshig gi rtog pa ste/ brgyad pa'o// de nas gzhan yang bshad pa ni// rdo rje sems dpa' dpal gyi lha'i// kun du sna tshogs mchog rnams kyi// phyag rgya thams cad rnam sprul pa'o// 
23b2(rgyud): sems dpa' sangs rgyas kun gyi dngos// rdo rje sems dpa' bde ba'i mchog/ gsang ba mchog gi dges pa ni// thams cad bdag nyid rtag tu bzhugs// bde ba kun gyi zhen pa dang // dngos
23b3(rgyud): grub thams cad rnam dag phyir// rdo rje sems dpa' bde ba'i mchog/ zla ba nya ltar rtsa dmar sku// 'dod chags kun la chags pa'i phyir// chags pa chen po bcom ldan 'das// dpal rdo rje sos
23b4(rgyud): dpa' phyag rgya 'di// dmar po sna tshogs 'bar ba'i 'od// khams gsum pa dag rin chen gzhan// sangs rgyas rin chen lta bu med rin chen sangs rgyas kun gyi che// dbu rgyan can ni de bas mchog
23b5(rgyud): gzhan gyi nor ni mi 'phrogs pas// lha'i chu yis dgra pa ste// mthu dang ngo bo nyid dag dang // rang bzhin gyis ni de grub pa'o// thed pa'i phreng ba'i dbu rgyan dang // sangs rgyas gtsug gi nor bu
23b6(rgyud): can kun nas nyon mongs 'jig rten dbang // mi 'byed la sogs de grub pa'o// rdo rje sems dpa' dpal 'byor pa// lha mo kun dang 'dus pa yis// kun du sna tshogs bskal bzang ba// mkha'
23b7(rgyud): 'gro ma ni thams cad 'grub// sangs rgyas rdo rje pad mo 'dzin// rdo rje nyi ma khams gsum pa// sangs rgyas btab rmongs byas spangs nas ni// las rnams kun la sbyor bar byed// phyag rgya 'di yis bdag
23b8(rgyud): na ni/ 'dod pa bzhin du 'gro 'ong ldeng // lha mo kun mchog dpal dang ldan// rdo rje sems dpa' rab tu 'grub// mchog tu dgo' ba rab tu sbyar// skal pa bzang po dpol rdo rje sems dpas// bde ba'i mchog
24a1(rgyud): rol pa zhes bya ba'i phyag rgya'o// g.yas dang g.yon pa'i sbyor ba yis// bde ba'i cha lugs gar byed cing // sems dpa' dkyil mo krung bcas nas// dpung rnams thams cad
24a2(rgyud): rab tu 'joms te dpal rdo rje semasang pa'i dkyil mo dkrung ngo // drwa pA'i kha dog 'dzum pa'i zhag/ dngos grub thams cad dag pa dang // pa ma'i 'dod chags rnam ngag phyir/ khA'i dbus ni
24a3(rgyud): dmar la dkar ta phyag mchog lo ma sngon po 'am// de bzhin byed pa'i dbang phyug dang // bde bar reg pa'i dbang phyug pas// dkar zhing ser ba'i rwa dang ldan// lha rdza saM sna tshogs kha reg
24a4(rgyud): mchog 'brar ba sna tshogs 'khrugs pa'i 'od phrad ma sna tshogs la gnas pa// thams cad dag par rab tu gnas// sangs rgyas pad mo la sogs phyag rgya mchog/ rin chen sna tshogs brgyan
24a5(rgyud): drang gos/ sangs rgyas thams cad 'dus pa yis/ kI mI 'byed la sogs rgya byin bzhin// bya ba dang ni zlog pa dang // 'phrog pa/ dag kyang ldag por mdzad// bdag la 'khyud pa'i phyag rgya
24a6(rgyud): yis te yan lag thams cad 'grogs par 'grub phyag rgya 'dri mi sro btab na ni// 'dod pa bzhin du 'gro 'ong ldeng // dpal ldan 'dod ba kun la dbang // rdo rje sems dpa' rab tu 'gru'o// 
24a7(rgyud): mchog tu dga' la rab sbyor ba// sprul pa bzang po dpal rdo rje bde ba'i mchog rol pa zhes bya ba'i phyag rgya'o// rnam pa sna tshogs dam tshig chags// bde ba 'bar ba'i gar byed pas// bdag la 'khyud
24a8(rgyud): pa'i phyag rgya mchog/ dbus kyi lha mo mchog chen po'o// phyag rgya 'di yis rdul 'byor pa// 'dod po bzhin du 'gro 'ong lding // khade chen dbang phyug dpal dang ldan// rdo rje sems dpa' rab tu 'grul
24b1(rgyud): mchog tu dga' la rab tu sbyor ba// skal pa bzang po dpal rdo rje sems dpa'i dam tshig bde ba'i mchog rol pa zhes bya ba'i phyag d+ha'o// seral khwa'i tshul dag tu// rdo rje khA l+li la bzung ste/ 
24b2(rgyud): bdag la 'khyud pa'i phyag rgya ni/ khang bcas rdo rje rgya khram mchog/ phyag rgya 'di yis btab nas ni// 'dod pa bzhin du 'gro 'ong lteng // rnal 'byor kun gyi dbang phyug rgyal// rdo rje sems dpa' rab tu
24b3(rgyud): 'grub tu mchog tu dga' ba la sbyor ba// bskal pa bzang po dpal rdo rje rnal 'byor bde ba'i mchog rol pa zhes bya ba'i phyag rgya'o// rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas kham por grub// bdag la 'khyud pa'i phyag rgya
24b4(rgyud): mis rdo rje sems dpa'i dpal sbyor ba// dbusakyi lha mchog chen po'o// phyag rgya 'dri yis nal 'byor pa// 'drod po bzhin du 'gro 'od ldeng // dpal ldan tshe dang gzhon grub pa// rdo rje sems
24b5(rgyud): dpa' rab tu 'grub / mchog tu dga' ba ra hU~M sbyor/ bskal pa bzang po dpal rdo rje bde ba'i mchog rol pa zhes bya ba'i phy-irgya'o// de la sogs pa mtha' mas mchog/ chos dbyings
24b6(rgyud): mnyam dang mi mnyam pa// nam mkha'i dbyings kyi mthas klas pa'i// rang 'byung phyag rgya sna tshogs rnams// nam mkha' kun gyi skyabs na dpal// dpal rdo rje sems dpa' la gnas te// grub pa'i dbang
24b7(rgyud): phyug rab bsgrubs pas// thams cad bdog nyid 'bar bar 'gyur// sangs rgyas thams cad mnyam par sbyor ba'i// mkha' 'gro sgyu ma bde ba'i mchog gi rtsa ba'i phyag rgya'i tshogs so// gtsug lag ji ltar
24b8(rgyud): rjes 'thun bi ra ta dpal tshogs phyag rgya gar ga gis// mda' bzhi yongs su 'phangs pa ni// bdud bzhi dag las rgyal bar 'gyur// tshangs pa chen po'i mgo dpal rdo rje mngal zhes bya ba'i phyag rgya'o// rkang pa/ 
25a1(rgyud): brdeg cing bab pa dang // gshibs te mchongs pa'i stabasnga dag gis// 'khor lo phyag rgyas skrod nas ni// khams gsum dgal 'chongs par 'gyur// dpal rdo rje
25a2(rgyud): mthu zhes bya ba'i phyag rgya'o// bya ba dang zlog pa dang // phrogs pa dag gi khyad par du// sna tshogs khyad par gar byed cing // khams gsum drug ni bsdu bar bya// dpal rdo rje gar gyi
25a3(rgyud): dbang phyug zhes bya ba'i phyag rgya'o// lcug ma gang yang rung bzung nas// bdag la'akhyud pa'i phyag rgya yis// bud med thams cad rtsed na ni// dpag bsam shing dag rab tu 'grub
25a4(rgyud): dpal rdo rje 'dod po'i lha mo zhes bya ba'i byig rgya'o// myang brtul ba ltar byas pas// drag po dbang po nye dbang bcas/ nyi zla gshin rje tshangs pa yi// 'jig rten gsum dag
25a5(rgyud): snyam par byed// dpal rdo rje rta drong zhes bya'i phyag rgya'o// sna'i myang ba'i rngub pa yis// drag po dbang po nye dbang bas nyi zla gshin rje tshangs pa yi// khams gsum yid ni bsrung
25a6(rgyud): par byed tedapal rdo rje brag mo zhes bya ba'i phyag rgya'o// mog tshungs pa lte ba yis// drag po dbang po nye dbang bcas// nyi zla gshin rje tshungs pa yis// 'jig rten gsum yang za bar byed/ 
25a7(rgyud): dpal rdo rje spyan nyi zla me zhes bya ba'i phyag rgya'o// thams cad bdag nyid myang ba yi// drag po dbang po nyid bang bcas// nyi zla gshin rje tshangs par bcas// thal bar 'gyur ba'ang 'tsho bor byed
25a8(rgyud): dpal rdo rje kun gyi bdag nyid khams gsum slar 'tsho ba zhes bya ba'i phyag rgya'o// gleng bu len pa'i tshul ston cing // ji ltar babs pa'i gar byed pas// tshangs pa nye dbang drag po
25b1(rgyud): bcas 'gro ba gsum dag dbang du byed// dpal rdo rje gleng bu'i dbang ces bya ba'i phyag rgya'o// pi wang len pa'i tshul ston cing // ji ltar babras pa'i gur byed pas// las rnams
25b2(rgyud): 'grub par rab 'byem dang // dngos grub ma lus myur du 'gru ga/ dpal rdo rje po wang po de bas rmongs par byed pa zhes bya ba'i phyag rgya'o// cang de'u tshul ston rnal 'byor pa// ji ltar
25b3(rgyud): babs pa'i gar byed pas// rims dang gdon dang drug zhen pa'i// sdug bsngal thams cad myur du sel// dpal rdo rje cang de'u srog bsngal thams cad sil ba zhes bya ba'i phyag rgya'o// 
25b4(rgyud): rdza rnga'i tshul skyon rnal 'byor pa// ji ltar thabs pa'i gar byed pas// gnas gsum dag ni ma lus pra// skad cig tsam gyis 'bebs par byed// dpal rdo rje rdza rngas myos par byed
25b5(rgyud): pA zhes bya ba'i phyag rgya'o// phyag rgya gar gyis mchod pa yis// mchod pa thams cad byas nas ni// rang 'byung gar gyi mchod pa rnams// ma lus lus pa med par 'gyu / 
25b6(rgyud): rims dang dug dang de byig dug byud// pra min gdon gyi gnod pa rnams// skor ba'i grwar rnams sna tshogs kyis// skad cig tsam gyis zhi bar 'gyur// drag po dbang po nyi dbang baHsa// 
25b7(rgyud): gshin rje tshangs bcas po// rgyas btob mongs byas zos pa dang // skad cig tsam gyis 'tshe bar byed// de la sogs pa mtha' yas mchog/ chos dbyings mnyam dang mi mnyam pa// nam mkha'i dbyings kyi mtha
25b8(rgyud): klas pa'i// rang 'byung lha mo'i phyag rgya rnams// nam mkha' kun gyi skabs na dpal// rdo rje sems dpa' la gnas te// dngos grub dbang phyug rab grub pas// thams cad bdag nyid 'bab par 'gyur/ 
26a1(rgyud): sangs rgyas thams cad mnyam sbyor ba// mkha' 'gro sgyu ma bde mchog gis// rab tu grub pa'i klu rnams kyis// bla na med pa'i dngos grub thob// de nas phyag rgya'i ye shes 'di'i
26a2(rgyud): dpal ldan rdo rje mchog glu// lus rnams thams cad rab bsgrub cing // srid pa shin tu bsgrub pa ni// rdo rje sems dpa' bde chen bskal bzang dpal// tshogs bdag lags skabs la rtogs par
26a3(rgyud): mdzad du gsol// kyi 'dra bzhin gshegs pa kun gyi bde ba mkha' 'gro sgyu ma sna tshogs bde ba'i mchog/ 'gro ba'i rgyud rnams rnam pa sna tshogs 'dul ba'i mchog 'grub pa'i bdag la grub pa
26a4(rgyud): mdzad du gsol/ a la la ho// de bzhin gshegs ba sbyor ba rnam pa sna tshogs gir rnams bstan du gsol// dza hU~M ba~M ho/ kye'o bde mchog bde bas zung rnam par sprul hUM snang bar mdzad du gsol/ 
26a5(rgyud): a la li sngo de bzhin ga shegs pa kun sna tshogs mkha' 'gro sgyu mas slob du ma bzung du gsol// sangs rgyas thams cad mnyam sbyor ba/ mkha' 'gro sbrum bang ba'i mchog/ kun du kun nas
26a6(rgyud): thams cad ni 'di nyid kyis ni myur du 'grub// sangs rgyas thams cad mnyam sbyor ba// mkha' 'gro ma'i rnal 'byor gyi dkyil 'khor gyi phyag rgya'o// rnal 'byor de nyid bcom ldan 'das// rdo rje sems dpa' ngo
26a7(rgyud): bzhin gshegs// thar pa thams cad rnam dag phyir// sangs rgyas phyag rgya dpal du gnas// don dam rnam par dag pa'i phyir// bcom gser gyi kha dog bzhin no// tshogs med la sogs chags chen phyir// dkar ni sa
26a8(rgyud): tshogs gsal ba'i mdangs// chos kyi rgyal srid rab bsgrubs pa// rin chen chos las lhag pa med// de bas theg chen byang chub sems// rgyal ba rdo rje rin chen can// g.yas pa'i 'the bong gung mo gnyis/ 
26b1(rgyud): g.yon pa'i khur tshur bcangs pa yis// so sor kun la reg pa ni// rtsa ba'i phyag rgya yin par glags// 'di na sangs rgyas thams cad kyi// shes rab pha rol phyin gsal yin// byang chub sems chen
26b2(rgyud): skye ba dang na chos kyi 'khor lo skor ba ste// phyag rgya 'di yis btab na ni// shos rab pha rol phyin pa'i tshul/ nam mkha'i dbyings kyi mthas klas par// rab tu skrag par 'gyur ba yin// byang chub
26b3(rgyud): soms ni skyed pa dang // chos kyi 'khor lo skor ba ste// sangs rgyas nyid du rig par bya// mchog tu dag po'i sangs rgyas so// glang gis ldan pa 'di mthong zhing // rnam pa kun du mchog byed pa/

50b5(rgyud): rgyas bti barmongs byas zos pa dang // thal bar gyur pa'ang 'tsho bor byed// dpal rdo rje he ru ka'i khro ma nyer zhes bya ba'i phyag rgya sgrom mo ste shes pa'o// rdo rje sems dpa' dpal sbyor bas/

50b7(rgyud): zhon nas ni// glang po thams cad nad med sos// nyam skye spro ldan myos par 'gyur// shi ba rdzas dmyo/ snga ma si ho/ 'di ni rnga ba ro bzla ba'i mchog/ bya rnams nad med 'tsho ba dang // me'i sri
50b8(rgyud): tu smra bar 'gyur te bya gso ba'i phyag rgya'o// rdo rje sems dpe'i dpal sbyor ba// sbyor ba kun la rjes chags na// shing rnams mi skam pa med cing // rtag tu me toga'abras bur ldan/ 
51a1(rgyud): shing rnams bskyed pa'i gtsug lag las// sbyor ba'i cho ga gang bshad pa// phyag rgya 'di yis thams cad ni// yid la bsam pa bzhin du 'grub// shing skyed pa'i phyag rgya shes pa'o/

51b6(rgyud): gnas gsum dag ni zlog par bya// nges par zlog pa'i thams cad kyi phyag rgya'o// thams cad 'debs dang nges paro 'debs/ kun 'debs gyen du 'debs pa'i bar// 'di dag 'phros pa'i phyag rgya'o// 
51b7(rgyud): gnas gsum dag kyang 'phrog par byed// 'phogs pa thams cad kyi phyag rgya'o// kun du kun nas thams cad kyi// rtag tu bdag nyid rnam pa kun// gzhu gzhu spyad kyi phyag rgya mchog/ mi 'gyur dam pa 'grub par
51b8(rgyud): 'gyur// dgra cha thams cad kyi phyag rgya shes pa'o// srin lag gnyis kyi nang du ni// 'the bong legs par bzhag par bya// de nas khu tshur bcings na ni// 'dzub mo legs par dgug par bya// rdo rje khu tshur
52a1(rgyud): dpal gyi phyag rgya'o// rdo rje sems dpa' dpal la gnas// las kyi dngos grub rab 'jam rnams// ma lus pa ni myur du 'grub// dpal rdo rje khu tshur gyi phyag rgya'o// rdo rje khu tshur legs
52a2(rgyud): bcings la ta bdag gi 'the bong nang du bzhug/ zhi ba'i las rnams rab 'grub pa// ma lus lus pa med par 'grub// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi khu tshur ro// rdo rje khu tshur khu tshur bcangs pa las
52a3(rgyud): 'the chung gnyis kyi rab rkyang nas// mkha' 'gro'i las rnams thams cad ni// ma lus lus pa med par 'grub// dpal rdo rje he ru ka'i khu tshur gyi phyag rgya'o// bdeg pa'i khu tshur bcangs pa las// mthe bong dag las
52a4(rgyud): gung mo gzhar// dpal pad mo khu tshur grub pa ste// thams cad dag pa'i las la sbyar// dpal pad mo khu tshur ro// khu tshur rdo rje rin chen mchog/ 'bebs pa thams cad yongs rdzogs pa/

52a8(rgyud): 'dzin pa dpal mnan nas// kun du grub pa yongs bkug ste// bdag gi spyad par de spyod do// sdig med stobs kyi ngo 'thon du// spyan ras gzigs dbang dpal mnan nas// kun du dpal mo yongs bkug ste/ 'das
52b1(rgyud): gi spyad pa de spyod do// sdig med stobs kyis ngo 'thon du// rdo rje nyi ma'i dpal mnan nas// kun du longs spyod yongs bkug ste// bdag gi spyad par de spyod do// sdig med stobs kyis ngo 'thon du
52b2(rgyud): rta mchog dam pa dpal mnan nas// thams cad dbang phyug yongs bkug ste// bdag gir spyad pa de spyod do// byang chub spyad pha rol phyin pa dang // grub dang gzungs dang sa rnams dang // rig dang phyag rgya
52b3(rgyud): rnams mnan nas// bdag gi spyad pa de spyod do// sdig med stobs kyis ngo 'thon du// dbang phyug dam pa mnan nas ni// mig gsum pa las gsum grub kug/ bdag gi spyad pa de spyod do// sdig med stobs kyis
52b4(rgyud): ngo 'thon du ta 'thu bo che yang mnan nas ni// stong las pad+ma mo yongs bkug ste// bdag gi spyad pa de spyod do// sdig med stobs kyis ngo 'thon du// skye dgu'i bdag po mnan nas ni// mos la sgrol ma
52b5(rgyud): yongs bkug nas// bdag gi spyad par de spyod do// sdig med stobs kyis ngo 'thon du// rab dga'i dbang phyug mnan nas ni// bdag gi bdag la dga' ba kug/ bdag gi spyad par de spyod do//

53a1(rgyud): thams cad dbang du 'gyur// dpal rdo rje 'gying ba'o// dpal ldan sna tshogs pad mo 'dzin// g.yon pa bdeg pa'i khu tshur dang // g.yas pa ldeng bar grub pa dang // sangs rgyas dbang phyug ting 'dzin byang // sangs
53a2(rgyud): rgyas thams cad 'phrar ba'o// g.yon pa dril bu sgra sgrogs cing // g.yas pa yi ni lag pa yis// rdo rje gyen du gsor zhing skor// sgyu ma thams cad 'byung bar 'gyur// dpal rdo rje sgyu ma'i dbang phyug ma'o// 
53a3(rgyud): g.yon pa g.yon pa'i rwa la gzhag/ lag pa g.yas pa'i 'dzub mo yis// rtse mo pad ma dam pa 'dzin// g.yas pa'i rwa la lag ngar gzhag/ mi dga' thams cad sel ba zhes bya ba'i phyag rgya'o// bdag gi

53a6(rgyud): kun du sna tshogs kyi// dam tshig rdog pa ste dgu pa'o// / de nas kun du sna tshogs kyis// phyag rgya shes pa sgrub pa ni// kun du sna tshogs sbyor ba yis// kun du sna tshogs bshad par bya// smin ma mig dang so
53a7(rgyud): 'chung khaM dang lus dang rga lag gis/ cha lugs bzhin du gar byed pas// phyag rgya thams cad yongs su grol// rdo rje sems dpa' dpal 'byor pa// lha mo kun dang 'dus pa ni// kun du sna tshogs skal bzang po/

53b4(rgyud): sprin chen thams cad kyi// bkod pa'i rab 'byam sna tshogs gyis// thams cad bdag nyid mchod par mdzad// dpal ldan g.yon pa 'gying dang bcas// dpal ldan lag pa g.yas pa yi//
